# Spec Audit Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Council Setup
Run three independent auditors with no shared findings until triage:
- Auditor A: requirement-first strict contract verification
- Auditor B: architecture consistency and cross-file behavior verification
- Auditor C: adversarial boundary and omission-focused verification

## Inputs
1. `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`
2. `quality/QUALITY.md`
3. `quality/CONTRACTS.md`
4. `quality/COVERAGE_MATRIX.md`
5. Relevant source files cited by each REQ

## Output Locations
- Auditor reports: `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor-1.md` .. `-3.md`
- Triage synthesis: `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-triage.md`
- Probe script: `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.sh`
- Probe output capture: `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.out.txt`

## Audit Procedure
1. Each auditor reviews all REQs independently and records per-REQ verdicts with code citations.
2. Triage compares overlaps, disagreements, and net-new findings.
3. Every confirmation or rejection using a probe must be executable evidence:
   - Write assertions in `triage_probes.sh` or `quality/mechanical/verify.sh`.
   - Execute probes and capture output file.
4. Classify each finding as:
   - `Real code bug`
   - `Spec gap`
   - `False positive`
   - `Needs follow-up`

## Mandatory Finding Fields
Each triage finding includes:
- `id` (`BUG-NNN` if confirmed)
- `requirement` (`REQ-NNN`)
- `source` (`code-spec` | `internal-prose` | `cross-source`)
- `severity` (`HIGH` | `MEDIUM` | `LOW`)
- `evidence` (file:line and/or probe output)
- `disposition` candidate

## Post-Triage Hooks
- Confirmed code bugs feed Phase 5 regression test workflow.
- Confirmed spec gaps feed requirement/spec update queue.
- Overturned code-review findings must be reconciled with regression artifacts.

# Quality Constitution: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Purpose
Quality in ZINC-FUSION-V16 means buyer-facing soybean oil procurement decisions are grounded in accurate, traceable, and operationally consistent data contracts across Supabase, API routes, dashboard rendering, and training gates.

Deming applies here as contract integrity built into route code, schema contracts, and quality artifacts before later review phases. Juran applies as fitness for procurement use: the system must preserve fallback behavior, route-envelope stability, and approval-gated model operations so Chris and Kevin do not consume misleading outputs. Crosby applies because preventing silent contract drift (status vocab mismatch, hidden overlay disablement, envelope divergence) is lower cost than downstream outage analysis and procurement mis-timing.

## Coverage Targets
| Subsystem | Target | Why |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `app/api/zl/*` forecast and intraday routes | 92% | These routes carry price, target-zone, and fallback contracts directly into decision surfaces; parity gaps are already observed in exploration. |
| `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx` and dashboard wiring | 90% | Target-zone visibility can be disabled even when data is present; this is high-impact on user interpretation. |
| `lib/server/*` ingest/snapshot/trusted-source utilities | 88% | Status normalization and trusted-source allowlists are cross-cutting and can silently drift. |
| `python/fusion/*` train/promote/pipeline gate paths | 90% | Explicit approval gates are a hard safety boundary for model execution and cloud promotion. |
| `supabase/migrations/*` ops and mkt contract tables | 85% | Schema-level vocabulary and fallback tables define runtime behavior and observability semantics. |
| `docs/*` operator-facing startup and policy docs | 75% | Documentation parity matters for operational correctness but is lower runtime criticality than core code paths. |

## Coverage Theater Prevention
The following are non-compliant test patterns for this repository:

- Asserting only HTTP status without validating payload contract fields (`ok`, `data`, `asOf`, `source`) where envelope semantics are required.
- Asserting that forecast/target arrays are non-empty without proving horizon normalization and per-route parity behavior.
- Testing ingestion telemetry by checking row existence only, without validating canonical status vocabulary alignment across SQL and TS writers.
- Testing chart rendering by mounting the component only, without checking that forecast-target overlay attachment path is enabled when target-zone data exists.
- Testing training gates by asserting dry-run returns a dict, without asserting non-approved non-dry behavior is blocked.
- Treating README existence as documentation quality; tests must assert repo policy alignment on prohibited hardcoded port guidance.

## Fitness-to-Purpose Scenarios
### Scenario 1: Intraday Fallback Contract Drift
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-001]

**What happened:** `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts` states a 15-minute then 1-minute fallback contract but currently executes only `mkt.price_15m` and always emits `source: "mkt.price_15m"`. During sparse 15-minute data windows, this permits empty/stale intraday payloads while a populated 1-minute table exists.

**The requirement:** Intraday route behavior must execute documented fallback semantics and emit source metadata that reflects the actual query path.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_001_intraday_route_contains_executable_1m_fallback`

### Scenario 2: Invisible Target Zones Despite Available Data
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-002]

**What happened:** Dashboard page fetches `targetZones` and passes them to `ZlCandlestickChart`, but `SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY = false` prevents `ForecastTargetsPrimitive` attachment. The architecture permits valid forecast-zone data to remain invisible to users.

**The requirement:** When target-zone data is supplied to chart boundary, overlay plumbing must be enabled or explicitly replaced by an equivalent visible projection.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.FitnessScenarioTests.test_scenario_2_forecast_overlay_gate_is_not_hard_disabled`

### Scenario 3: Divergent Forecast Target API Envelopes
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-002]

**What happened:** `/api/zl/target-zones` uses a typed envelope while `/api/zl/forecast-targets` uses `{asOfDate, targets}` and route-specific error shape. This permits parser duplication and inconsistent error handling across consumers of equivalent domain data.

**The requirement:** Forecast-target routes must share one canonical response envelope or provide explicit typed adapters documenting differences.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_002_forecast_target_routes_share_api_envelope_contract`

### Scenario 4: Ingest Status Vocabulary Fragmentation
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-003]

**What happened:** SQL jobs write lower-case `running/ok/failed` while TS helper writes upper-case `RUNNING/SUCCESS/FAILED` to `ops.ingest_run.status`. This permits split analytics filters and inconsistent alert logic.

**The requirement:** All writers to `ops.ingest_run.status` must use one canonical status vocabulary.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_003_ingest_status_vocab_is_canonical_across_writers`

### Scenario 5: Unauthorized Model Execution
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-004]

**What happened:** Train and promote phases are safety-critical operations. If approval gates are bypassed in non-dry runs, model artifacts or cloud tables can mutate without explicit operator authorization.

**The requirement:** Non-dry `train` and `promote` execution requires explicit approval and emits a blocking error when approval is absent.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_004_train_phase_requires_explicit_approval`

### Scenario 6: Runtime External Pull Coupling on Read Paths
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-006]

**What happened:** AI-first routes still perform request-time trusted-market pulls before snapshot fallback. Third-party latency/outage can cascade into user-facing API delays.

**The requirement:** Runtime read-path external pulls must either be bounded with explicit fallback semantics or isolated behind snapshot-first behavior with clear degraded metadata.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.FitnessScenarioTests.test_scenario_6_routes_document_snapshot_and_trusted_pull_order`

### Scenario 7: Snapshot Trust Boundary Drift
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-004]

**What happened:** `TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES` defines a strict allowlist. If producers are added without allowlist updates, snapshots fail closed and AI cards silently lose expected data.

**The requirement:** Any new snapshot source identifier must be updated in the trust allowlist in the same change as producer wiring.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.BoundaryAndEdgeCaseTests.test_boundary_trusted_snapshot_sources_are_exactly_expected_set`

### Scenario 8: Operator Guidance Drift
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-012]

**What happened:** Root README includes starter-template startup guidance including localhost:3000 while authority docs prohibit hardcoded port assumptions. This can mislead operators and parity validation steps.

**The requirement:** Operator-facing docs must not reintroduce prohibited startup assumptions that conflict with V16 authority rules.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.FitnessScenarioTests.test_scenario_8_readme_drift_is_detectable`

## AI Session Quality Discipline
1. Read `quality/QUALITY.md`, `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`, and `quality/COVERAGE_MATRIX.md` before modifying implementation.
2. Preserve `Pattern` fields on all pattern-tagged REQs in both markdown and manifest artifacts.
3. Do not modify files outside `quality/` during quality playbook phase execution.
4. For enumeration/allowlist claims, use mechanical extraction artifacts under `quality/mechanical/` before writing conclusions.
5. Run `quality/mechanical/verify.sh` after changing any requirement tied to enumeration or dispatch completeness.
6. Update `quality/PROGRESS.md` artifact inventory in the same change as generated artifact updates.

## The Human Gate
- Approving training and cloud promotion execution beyond dry-run gates.
- Accepting temporary contract divergence when external dependencies or release constraints require staged remediation.
- Deciding rollout timing for envelope-contract convergence across independently consumed API surfaces.
- Prioritizing UX tradeoffs for chart overlays and degraded-mode messaging under live-feed outages.

## Contract Inventory
### `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts`
1. `[API]` `GET()` advertises a two-step fallback contract (15m then 1m) and must keep declaration and executable path aligned. (`app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:16-23`)
2. `[OBSERVABILITY]` `ApiEnvelope.source` must identify the actual table path used for response payload. (`app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:41-46`)

### `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql`
3. `[INVARIANT]` `mkt.price_15m` and `mkt.price_1m` coexist as eligible intraday data sources; route behavior must remain consistent with this schema capability. (`supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql:18-19`)

### `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts` and `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts`
4. `[API]` Forecast-target surfaces represent the same domain payload and must converge on one stable envelope or explicit typed adapter contracts. (`app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:80-87`, `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:103-106`)
5. `[INVARIANT]` Horizon normalization behavior (`AG_HORIZON_DAYS`, `LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP`, `normalizeHorizon`) must remain equivalent across all forecast-target routes. (`app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:7-24`, `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:16-33`, `app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts:7-24`)

### `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx` and dashboard page wiring
6. `[API]` Chart receives `targetZones` from dashboard page and must render equivalent target-zone signal when data exists. (`app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx:12-33`, `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:40`, `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:257-269`)
7. `[LIFECYCLE]` Primitive attach/detach lifecycle must mirror feature gates to avoid silent rendering path disablement. (`components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:253-266`, `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:332-337`)

### `ops.ingest_run` schema and writers
8. `[OBSERVABILITY]` All writers to `ops.ingest_run.status` must share one canonical status vocabulary for deterministic analytics and alerting. (`supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql:3-8`, `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3-4`, `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:55-57`)
9. `[LIFECYCLE]` Run lifecycle semantics (`start`, terminal success/failure, timestamps, records count) must preserve one run-id progression contract. (`lib/server/ingest-run.ts:6-26`, `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:28-61`)

### Training and promotion gates
10. `[SECURITY]` Non-dry training and cloud promotion execution is approval-gated; calls without explicit approval must fail closed. (`python/fusion/pipeline.py:46-58`, `python/fusion/train_models.py:770-773`, `python/fusion/promote_to_cloud.py:172-173`)
11. `[INVARIANT]` Pipeline phase dispatcher must preserve approval flags through `run_phase` boundary to downstream stage functions. (`python/fusion/pipeline.py:46-58`)

### Snapshot trust and external pull coupling
12. `[INVARIANT]` Snapshot intake requires metadata and trusted-source allowlist membership; untrusted identifiers fail closed. (`lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts:21-27`, `lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts:41-50`)
13. `[API]` AI-first card routes using runtime trusted-market pulls must maintain explicit fallback to snapshots and degraded-mode visibility when pulls fail. (`app/api/strategy/posture/route.ts:142-169`, `app/api/sentiment/overview/route.ts:188-193`, `lib/server/trusted-market-sources.ts:139-146`)

### Documentation alignment
14. `[DOCS]` Operator startup and environment instructions must align with V16 authority docs and avoid prohibited hardcoded-port assumptions. (`README.md:1-4`, `README.md:95`, `AGENTS.md:53`)

     1	import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
     2	
     3	import { requireAuthenticatedApiRequest } from "@/lib/server/auth-guards";
     4	import { createSupabaseAdminClient } from "@/lib/server/supabase-admin";
     5	import type { ApiEnvelope, TargetZone } from "@/lib/contracts/api";
     6	
     7	const AG_HORIZON_DAYS = [30, 90, 180] as const;
     8	const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP: Record<number, (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number]> = {
     9	  7: 30,
    10	  14: 90,
    11	  30: 180,
    12	};
    13	
    14	function normalizeHorizon(row: {
    15	  horizon_days: number;
    16	  model_version: string | null;
    17	}): number | null {
    18	  if (AG_HORIZON_DAYS.includes(row.horizon_days as (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number])) {
    19	    return row.horizon_days;
    20	  }
    21	  if (row.model_version?.startsWith("trusted-fill-v1")) {
    22	    return LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP[row.horizon_days] ?? null;
    23	  }
    24	  return null;
    25	}
    26	
    27	export async function GET() {
    28	  try {
    29	    const unauthorized = await requireAuthenticatedApiRequest();
    30	    if (unauthorized) {
    31	      return unauthorized;
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();
    35	
    36	    // Get the latest target zones (most recent forecast_date, all horizons)
    37	    const { data: rows, error } = await supabase
    38	      .schema("forecasts")
    39	      .from("target_zones")
    40	      .select("horizon_days, p30, p50, p70, model_version, generated_at, forecast_date")
    41	      .order("forecast_date", { ascending: false })
    42	      .limit(20);
    43	
    44	    if (error) {
    45	      return NextResponse.json(
    46	        { ok: false, data: [], asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: error.message },
    47	        { status: 500 },
    48	      );
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    if (!rows || rows.length === 0) {
    52	      const envelope: ApiEnvelope<TargetZone[]> = {
    53	        ok: true,
    54	        data: [],
    55	        asOf: new Date().toISOString(),
    56	        source: "forecasts.target_zones",
    57	      };
    58	      return NextResponse.json(envelope);
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    // Get the latest forecast_date and filter to only that date's zones
    62	    const latestDate = rows[0].forecast_date;
    63	    const latestZones = rows.filter((r) => r.forecast_date === latestDate);
    64	
    65	    const deduped = new Map<number, TargetZone>();
    66	    for (const row of latestZones) {
    67	      const horizonDays = normalizeHorizon(row);
    68	      if (!horizonDays) continue;
    69	      if (deduped.has(horizonDays)) continue;
    70	      deduped.set(horizonDays, {
    71	        horizonDays,
    72	        p30: Number(row.p30),
    73	        p50: Number(row.p50),
    74	        p70: Number(row.p70),
    75	        generatedAt: row.generated_at,
    76	      });
    77	    }
    78	    const zones = [...deduped.values()].sort((a, b) => a.horizonDays - b.horizonDays);
    79	
    80	    const envelope: ApiEnvelope<TargetZone[]> = {
    81	      ok: true,
    82	      data: zones,
    83	      asOf: new Date().toISOString(),
    84	      source: "forecasts.target_zones",
    85	    };
    86	
    87	    return NextResponse.json(envelope);
    88	  } catch (err) {
    89	    return NextResponse.json(
    90	      { ok: false, data: [], asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: String(err) },
    91	      { status: 500 },
    92	    );
    93	  }
    94	}

     1	import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
     2	
     3	import { requireAuthenticatedApiRequest } from "@/lib/server/auth-guards";
     4	import { createSupabaseAdminClient } from "@/lib/server/supabase-admin";
     5	
     6	type ForecastTarget = {
     7	  id: string;
     8	  horizonDays: number;
     9	  horizonLabel: string;
    10	  priceLow: number;
    11	  priceHigh: number;
    12	  oofPrice: number;
    13	  coveragePct: number | null;
    14	};
    15	
    16	const AG_HORIZON_DAYS = [30, 90, 180] as const;
    17	const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP: Record<number, (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number]> = {
    18	  7: 30,
    19	  14: 90,
    20	  30: 180,
    21	};
    22	
    23	function normalizeHorizon(row: {
    24	  horizon_days: number;
    25	  model_version: string | null;
    26	}): number | null {
    27	  if (AG_HORIZON_DAYS.includes(row.horizon_days as (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number])) {
    28	    return row.horizon_days;
    29	  }
    30	  if (row.model_version?.startsWith("trusted-fill-v1")) {
    31	    return LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP[row.horizon_days] ?? null;
    32	  }
    33	  return null;
    34	}
    35	
    36	function horizonLabel(days: number): string {
    37	  if (days === 30) return "1M";
    38	  if (days === 90) return "3M";
    39	  if (days === 180) return "6M";
    40	  return `${days}d`;
    41	}
    42	
    43	export async function GET() {
    44	  try {
    45	    const unauthorized = await requireAuthenticatedApiRequest();
    46	    if (unauthorized) {
    47	      return unauthorized;
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();
    51	
    52	    const { data: rows, error } = await supabase
    53	      .schema("forecasts")
    54	      .from("target_zones")
    55	      .select("forecast_date, horizon_days, p30, p50, p70, model_version")
    56	      .order("forecast_date", { ascending: false })
    57	      .limit(60);
    58	
    59	    if (error) {
    60	      return NextResponse.json(
    61	        { error: error.message, asOfDate: null, targets: [] as ForecastTarget[] },
    62	        { status: 500 },
    63	      );
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    if (!rows || rows.length === 0) {
    67	      return NextResponse.json({
    68	        asOfDate: null,
    69	        targets: [] as ForecastTarget[],
    70	      });
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    const asOfDate = rows[0].forecast_date;
    74	    const latestRows = rows.filter((r) => r.forecast_date === asOfDate);
    75	    const deduped = new Map<number, ForecastTarget>();
    76	    for (const row of latestRows) {
    77	      const horizonDays = normalizeHorizon(row);
    78	      if (!horizonDays) continue;
    79	      if (deduped.has(horizonDays)) continue;
    80	      deduped.set(horizonDays, {
    81	        id: `${row.forecast_date}-${horizonDays}`,
    82	        horizonDays,
    83	        horizonLabel: horizonLabel(horizonDays),
    84	        priceLow: Number(row.p30),
    85	        priceHigh: Number(row.p70),
    86	        oofPrice: Number(row.p50),
    87	        coveragePct: null,
    88	      });
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    const targets: ForecastTarget[] = [...deduped.values()]
    92	      .sort((a, b) => a.horizonDays - b.horizonDays)
    93	      .map((r) => ({
    94	        id: r.id,
    95	        horizonDays: r.horizonDays,
    96	        horizonLabel: r.horizonLabel,
    97	        priceLow: r.priceLow,
    98	        priceHigh: r.priceHigh,
    99	        oofPrice: r.oofPrice,
   100	        coveragePct: r.coveragePct,
   101	      }));
   102	
   103	    return NextResponse.json({
   104	      asOfDate,
   105	      targets,
   106	    });
   107	  } catch (err) {
   108	    return NextResponse.json(
   109	      { error: String(err), asOfDate: null, targets: [] as ForecastTarget[] },
   110	      { status: 500 },
   111	    );
   112	  }
   113	}

     3	import { requireAuthenticatedApiRequest } from "@/lib/server/auth-guards";
     4	import { createSupabaseAdminClient } from "@/lib/server/supabase-admin";
     5	import type { ApiEnvelope, ForecastSummary } from "@/lib/contracts/api";
     6	
     7	const AG_HORIZON_DAYS = [30, 90, 180] as const;
     8	const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP: Record<number, (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number]> = {
     9	  7: 30,
    10	  14: 90,
    11	  30: 180,
    12	};
    13	
    14	function normalizeHorizon(row: {
    15	  horizon_days: number;
    16	  model_version: string | null;
    17	}): number | null {
    18	  if (AG_HORIZON_DAYS.includes(row.horizon_days as (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number])) {
    19	    return row.horizon_days;
    20	  }
    21	  if (row.model_version?.startsWith("trusted-fill-v1")) {
    22	    return LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP[row.horizon_days] ?? null;
    23	  }
    24	  return null;
    25	}
    26	
    27	export async function GET() {
    28	  try {
    29	    const unauthorized = await requireAuthenticatedApiRequest();
    30	    if (unauthorized) {
    31	      return unauthorized;
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();
    35	
    36	    // Get the latest forecast summaries (most recent forecast_date)
    37	    const { data: rows, error } = await supabase
    38	      .schema("forecasts")
    39	      .from("forecast_summary_1d")
    40	      .select("horizon_days, predicted_price, hit_probability, model_version, forecast_date")
    41	      .order("forecast_date", { ascending: false })
    42	      .limit(20);
    43	
    44	    if (error) {
    45	      return NextResponse.json(
    46	        { ok: false, data: [], asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: error.message },
    47	        { status: 500 },
    48	      );
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    if (!rows || rows.length === 0) {
    52	      const envelope: ApiEnvelope<ForecastSummary[]> = {
    53	        ok: true,
    54	        data: [],
    55	        asOf: new Date().toISOString(),
    56	        source: "forecasts.forecast_summary_1d",
    57	      };
    58	      return NextResponse.json(envelope);
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    // Filter to the latest forecast_date only
    62	    const latestDate = rows[0].forecast_date;
    63	    const latestRows = rows.filter((r) => r.forecast_date === latestDate);
    64	
    65	    const deduped = new Map<number, ForecastSummary>();
    66	    for (const row of latestRows) {
    67	      const horizonDays = normalizeHorizon(row);
    68	      if (!horizonDays) continue;
    69	      if (deduped.has(horizonDays)) continue;
    70	      deduped.set(horizonDays, {
    71	        horizonDays,
    72	        predictedPrice: Number(row.predicted_price),
    73	        hitProbability: Number(row.hit_probability ?? 0),
    74	        modelVersion: row.model_version,
    75	      });
    76	    }
    77	    const forecasts = [...deduped.values()].sort((a, b) => a.horizonDays - b.horizonDays);
    78	
    79	    const envelope: ApiEnvelope<ForecastSummary[]> = {
    80	      ok: true,
    81	      data: forecasts,
    82	      asOf: new Date().toISOString(),
    83	      source: "forecasts.forecast_summary_1d",
    84	    };
    85	
    86	    return NextResponse.json(envelope);
    87	  } catch (err) {
    88	    return NextResponse.json(
    89	      { ok: false, data: [], asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: String(err) },
    90	      { status: 500 },
    91	    );
    92	  }
    93	}

     1	import type { SupabaseClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";
     2	
     3	export type IngestRunStatus = "RUNNING" | "SUCCESS" | "FAILED";
     4	
     5	export async function logIngestRunStart(
     6	  client: SupabaseClient,
     7	  jobName: string,
     8	  source: string,
     9	): Promise<string> {
    10	  const runId = crypto.randomUUID();
    11	
    12	  try {
    13	    await client.schema("ops").from("ingest_run").insert({
    14	      run_id: runId,
    15	      job_name: jobName,
    16	      source,
    17	      status: "RUNNING",
    18	      started_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    19	      records_upserted: 0,
    20	    });
    21	  } catch (error) {
    22	    console.error("Failed to write ops.ingest_run start record", error);
    23	  }
    24	
    25	  return runId;
    26	}
    27	
    28	export async function logIngestRunFinish(
    29	  client: SupabaseClient,
    30	  runId: string,
    31	  recordsUpserted: number,
    32	): Promise<void> {
    33	  try {
    34	    await client
    35	      .schema("ops")
    36	      .from("ingest_run")
    37	      .update({
    38	        status: "SUCCESS",
    39	        finished_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    40	        records_upserted: recordsUpserted,
    41	      })
    42	      .eq("run_id", runId);
    43	  } catch (error) {
    44	    console.error("Failed to write ops.ingest_run success record", error);
    45	  }
    46	}
    47	
    48	export async function logIngestRunFailure(
    49	  client: SupabaseClient,
    50	  runId: string,
    51	  errorMessage: string,
    52	): Promise<void> {
    53	  try {
    54	    await client
    55	      .schema("ops")
    56	      .from("ingest_run")
    57	      .update({
    58	        status: "FAILED",
    59	        finished_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    60	        error_message: errorMessage.slice(0, 2000),
    61	      })
    62	      .eq("run_id", runId);
    63	  } catch (error) {
    64	    console.error("Failed to write ops.ingest_run failure record", error);
    65	  }
    66	}

    17	PhaseFn = Callable[..., dict[str, object]]
    18	
    19	PHASE_MAP: dict[str, PhaseFn] = {
    20	    "matrix": build_matrix.run,
    21	    "specialists": generate_specialist_features.run,
    22	    "signals": generate_specialist_signals.run,
    23	    "train-readiness": training_readiness_gate.run,
    24	    "train": train_models.run,

    28	    "target-zones": generate_target_zones.run,
    29	    "promote": promote_to_cloud.run,
    30	}
    31	
    32	PIPELINE_ORDER = [
    33	    "matrix",
    34	    "specialists",
    35	    "signals",
    36	    "train-readiness",
    37	    "train",
    38	    "forecast",
    39	    "garch",
    40	    "monte-carlo",
    41	    "target-zones",
    42	    "promote",
    43	]
    44	
    45	
    46	def run_phase(
    47	    name: str,
    48	    *,
    49	    dry_run: bool,
    50	    approve_training: bool,
    51	    approve_promotion: bool,
    52	) -> dict[str, object]:
    53	    fn = PHASE_MAP[name]
    54	    if name == "train":
    55	        return fn(dry_run=dry_run, approved=approve_training)
    56	    if name == "promote":
    57	        return fn(dry_run=dry_run or not approve_promotion, approved=approve_promotion)
    58	    return fn(dry_run=dry_run)
    59	
    60	
    61	def main() -> None:
    62	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="ZINC Fusion v16 pipeline runner")
    63	    parser.add_argument("--all", action="store_true", help="Run all phases in pipeline order")
    64	    parser.add_argument("--phase", choices=PIPELINE_ORDER, help="Run one phase")
    65	    parser.add_argument("--dry-run", action="store_true", help="Show intent only, no writes")
    66	    parser.add_argument(
    67	        "--approve-training",
    68	        action="store_true",
    69	        help="Explicit training approval gate for non-dry-run train phase",
    70	    )
    71	    parser.add_argument(
    72	        "--approve-promotion",
    73	        action="store_true",
    74	        help="Explicit cloud promotion approval gate for non-dry-run promote phase",
    75	    )
    76	    args = parser.parse_args()
    77	
    78	    selected: list[str]
    79	    if args.all:
    80	        selected = PIPELINE_ORDER
    81	    elif args.phase:
    82	        selected = [args.phase]
    83	    else:
    84	        parser.error("Select --all or --phase")
    85	
    86	    for phase in selected:
    87	        result = run_phase(
    88	            phase,
    89	            dry_run=args.dry_run,
    90	            approve_training=args.approve_training,
    91	            approve_promotion=args.approve_promotion,
    92	        )
    93	        print(result)
    94	
    95	
    96	if __name__ == "__main__":
    97	    main()

   131	        (row["trade_date"], _json_from_row(row, exclude={"trade_date"}))

   145	    return len(rows)

   147	
   148	def run(*, dry_run: bool = True, approved: bool = False) -> dict[str, object]:
   149	    matrix = _validate_matrix()
   150	    specialists = {specialist: _validate_specialist(specialist) for specialist in SPECIALISTS}
   151	    signals = _validate_signals()
   152	
   153	    payload: dict[str, object] = {
   154	        "phase": "promote",
   155	        "dry_run": dry_run,
   156	        "approved": approved,
   157	        "reads": [
   158	            str(matrix_path()),
   159	            str(signals_path()),
   160	            *[str(specialist_features_path(specialist)) for specialist in SPECIALISTS],
   161	        ],
   162	        "writes": ["training.matrix_1d", "training.specialist_signals_1d", *[f"training.specialist_features_{s}" for s in SPECIALISTS]],
   163	        "target_columns_stripped_from_matrix_payload": target_columns(matrix.columns),
   164	        "matrix_rows": int(len(matrix)),
   165	        "signal_rows": int(len(signals)),
   166	        "specialist_rows": {specialist: int(len(frame)) for specialist, frame in specialists.items()},
   167	        "status": "dry-run" if dry_run else "pending",
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    if dry_run:
   171	        return payload
   172	    if not approved:
   173	        raise PromotionApprovalError("Cloud promotion requires explicit approval. Pass approved=True or --execute.")
   174	
   175	    db_url = resolve_cloud_db_url()
   176	    if not db_url:
   177	        raise RuntimeError(
   178	            "Cloud DB URL is not set. Configure DATABASE_URL, SUPABASE_DB_URL, POSTGRES_URL_NON_POOLING, or SUPABASE_POOLER_URL."
   179	        )
   180	
   181	    with psycopg2.connect(db_url, connect_timeout=10, application_name="fusion_promote_to_cloud") as conn:
   182	        with conn.cursor() as cur:
   183	            promoted = {
   184	                "training.matrix_1d": _promote_matrix(cur, matrix),
   185	                "training.specialist_signals_1d": _promote_signals(cur, signals),
   186	            }
   187	            for specialist, frame in specialists.items():
   188	                promoted[f"training.specialist_features_{specialist}"] = _promote_specialist(cur, specialist, frame)
   189	
   190	    payload["status"] = "ok"
   191	    payload["promoted_rows"] = promoted
   192	    payload["promoted_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
   193	    return payload
   194	
   195	
   196	def main() -> None:
   197	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Validate and promote local V16 training artifacts to cloud Supabase")
   198	    parser.add_argument("--dry-run", action="store_true", default=True, help="Validate local artifacts without cloud writes")
   199	    parser.add_argument("--execute", action="store_true", help="Perform approved cloud promotion")
   200	    args = parser.parse_args()
   201	
   202	    result = run(dry_run=not args.execute, approved=args.execute)

    97	function buildProvenance(
    98	  generatedAt: string,
    99	  tradeDate: string | null,
   100	  cardKey: keyof StrategyCards,
   101	  trustedUrls: string[],
   102	): AiCardProvenance {
   103	  return {
   104	    asOf: tradeDate ?? generatedAt,
   105	    generatedAt,
   106	    method: "verified-db-and-trusted-market-pull",
   107	    sourceFeeds: [
   108	      "analytics.market_posture",
   109	      "analytics.dashboard_metrics",
   110	      "analytics.driver_attribution_1d",
   111	      ...trustedUrls,
   112	    ],
   113	    sourceRecords: [
   114	      {
   115	        source: "analytics.market_posture",
   116	        table: "analytics.market_posture",
   117	        recordHint: tradeDate ? `trade_date=${tradeDate}` : "latest row",
   118	        observedAt: tradeDate ?? undefined,
   119	      },
   120	      {
   121	        source: "analytics.driver_attribution_1d",
   122	        table: "analytics.driver_attribution_1d",
   123	        recordHint: `card=${cardKey}`,
   124	        observedAt: tradeDate ?? generatedAt,
   125	      },
   126	    ],
   127	    notes: [
   128	      "Buyer posture is interpreted from verified table and market-source pulls.",
   129	      "Hard stop is applied when required driver or market evidence is missing.",
   130	    ],
   131	  };
   132	}
   133	
   134	export async function GET() {
   135	  try {
   136	    const unauthorized = await requireAuthenticatedApiRequest();
   137	    if (unauthorized) {
   138	      return unauthorized;
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();
   142	    const aiSnapshot = await readAiSnapshot<StrategyAiSnapshot>(
   143	      "app/config/strategy-posture-ai.json",
   144	    );
   145	    const trustedMarket = await fetchTrustedMarketSnapshot();
   146	    const trustedUrls = uniqueTrustedMarketUrls(trustedMarket);
   147	
   148	    const [{ data: row, error }, { data: attributionRows }, { data: metricRows }] = await Promise.all([
   149	      supabase
   150	        .schema("analytics")
   151	        .from("market_posture")
   152	        .select("posture, rationale, trade_date")
   153	        .order("trade_date", { ascending: false })
   154	        .limit(1)
   155	        .maybeSingle(),
   156	      supabase
   157	        .schema("analytics")
   158	        .from("driver_attribution_1d")
   159	        .select("trade_date, rank, factor, contribution")
   160	        .order("trade_date", { ascending: false })
   161	        .order("rank", { ascending: true })
   162	        .limit(40),
   163	      supabase
   164	        .schema("analytics")
   165	        .from("dashboard_metrics")
   166	        .select("trade_date, metric_key, metric_value")
   167	        .order("trade_date", { ascending: false })
   168	        .limit(300),
   169	    ]);
   170	
   171	    if (error) {
   172	      return NextResponse.json(
   173	        { ok: false, data: null, asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: error.message },
   174	        { status: 500 },
   175	      );
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    const latestAttrDate = attributionRows?.[0]?.trade_date ?? null;
   179	    const latestAttr = (attributionRows ?? []).filter((r) => r.trade_date === latestAttrDate);
   180	    const topFactors = latestAttr
   181	      .slice(0, 4)
   182	      .map((r) => `${String(r.factor)} (${Number(r.contribution).toFixed(2)})`);
   183	
   184	    const latestMetricDate = metricRows?.[0]?.trade_date ?? null;
   185	    const latestMetrics = (metricRows ?? []).filter((r) => r.trade_date === latestMetricDate);
   186	    const metricMap = new Map<string, number>();
   187	    for (const rowMetric of latestMetrics) {
   188	      const n = Number(rowMetric.metric_value);
   189	      if (Number.isFinite(n)) {
   190	        metricMap.set(String(rowMetric.metric_key).toLowerCase(), n);
   191	      }
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    const dbVix = metricMap.get("vix_value") ?? null;
   195	    const dbOvx = metricMap.get("ovx_value") ?? null;
   196	    const dbCl5d = metricMap.get("cl_change_5d") ?? metricMap.get("crude_oil_change_5d") ?? null;
   197	    const liveVix = trustedMarket.vix.value ?? dbVix;
   198	    const liveOvx = trustedMarket.ovx.value ?? dbOvx;
   199	    const liveCl5d = trustedMarket.cl.change5d ?? dbCl5d;
   200	
   201	    const dbPosture: StrategyPosture | null = row
   202	      ? {
   203	          posture: row.posture as StrategyPosture["posture"],
   204	          rationale: row.rationale ?? "",
   205	          updatedAt: row.trade_date ?? new Date().toISOString(),
   206	        }
   207	      : null;
   208	
   209	    const posture: StrategyPosture | null = aiSnapshot?.posture ?? dbPosture;
   210	    const generatedAt = aiSnapshot?.generatedAt ?? new Date().toISOString();
   211	    const tradeDate = row?.trade_date ?? posture?.updatedAt ?? null;
   212	    const stagedExecutionBias =
   213	      posture?.posture === "ACCUMULATE"
   214	        ? "Staged accumulation remains favored."
   215	        : posture?.posture === "WAIT"
   216	          ? "Hold execution optionality and avoid urgency."
   217	          : "Defer new exposure until risk compression is visible.";
   218	    const volatilityLine =
   219	      liveVix !== null && liveOvx !== null
   220	        ? `VIX ${liveVix.toFixed(2)} and OVX ${liveOvx.toFixed(2)} remain active volatility constraints.`
   221	        : "Hard stop: verified VIX/OVX volatility reads are unavailable.";
   222	    const crudeLine =
   223	      liveCl5d !== null
   224	        ? `CL 5-day change is ${(liveCl5d * 100).toFixed(2)}%, informing near-term pass-through risk.`
   225	        : "Hard stop: verified CL 5-day change is unavailable.";
   226	    const topFactorLine =
   227	      topFactors.length > 0
   228	        ? `Latest verified attribution stack: ${topFactors.join(", ")}.`
   229	        : "Hard stop: no verified attribution rows available in analytics.driver_attribution_1d.";
   230	    const noTrustedFeeds =
   231	      liveVix === null && liveOvx === null && liveCl5d === null;
   232	
   233	    const fallbackCards: StrategyCards = {
   234	      contractImpactCalculator: {
   235	        title: "Contract Impact Calculator",
   236	        body: noTrustedFeeds
   237	          ? "Hard stop: trusted market evidence from Yahoo/FRED is unavailable, so contract-impact guidance is blocked."
   238	          : `${stagedExecutionBias} ${volatilityLine} ${crudeLine}`,
   239	        strategicSpecialInstructions: STRATEGY_INSTRUCTIONS.contractImpactCalculator,
   240	        provenance: buildProvenance(generatedAt, tradeDate, "contractImpactCalculator", trustedUrls),
   241	      },
   242	      factorWaterfall: {
   243	        title: "Factor Waterfall",
   244	        body: topFactorLine,
   245	        strategicSpecialInstructions: STRATEGY_INSTRUCTIONS.factorWaterfall,
   246	        provenance: buildProvenance(generatedAt, tradeDate, "factorWaterfall", trustedUrls),
   247	      },
   248	      riskMetrics: {
   249	        title: "Risk Metrics",
   250	        body: noTrustedFeeds
   251	          ? "Hard stop: trusted volatility and crude metrics are unavailable; buyer risk-math output is blocked until verified feeds recover."
   252	          : `${volatilityLine} ${crudeLine} Decision-latency risk should be prioritized over single-window execution risk when these channels remain elevated.`,
   253	        strategicSpecialInstructions: STRATEGY_INSTRUCTIONS.riskMetrics,
   254	        provenance: buildProvenance(generatedAt, tradeDate, "riskMetrics", trustedUrls),
   255	      },
   256	    };
   257	
   258	    const rawCards = aiSnapshot?.cards ?? fallbackCards;
   259	    const cards: StrategyCards = {
   260	      contractImpactCalculator: {
   261	        ...fallbackCards.contractImpactCalculator,
   262	        ...rawCards.contractImpactCalculator,
   263	        strategicSpecialInstructions:
   264	          rawCards.contractImpactCalculator?.strategicSpecialInstructions ??
   265	          STRATEGY_INSTRUCTIONS.contractImpactCalculator,
   266	        provenance:
   267	          rawCards.contractImpactCalculator?.provenance ??
   268	          buildProvenance(generatedAt, tradeDate, "contractImpactCalculator", trustedUrls),
   269	      },
   270	      factorWaterfall: {
   271	        ...fallbackCards.factorWaterfall,
   272	        ...rawCards.factorWaterfall,
   273	        strategicSpecialInstructions:
   274	          rawCards.factorWaterfall?.strategicSpecialInstructions ??
   275	          STRATEGY_INSTRUCTIONS.factorWaterfall,
   276	        provenance:
   277	          rawCards.factorWaterfall?.provenance ??
   278	          buildProvenance(generatedAt, tradeDate, "factorWaterfall", trustedUrls),
   279	      },
   280	      riskMetrics: {
   281	        ...fallbackCards.riskMetrics,
   282	        ...rawCards.riskMetrics,
   283	        strategicSpecialInstructions:
   284	          rawCards.riskMetrics?.strategicSpecialInstructions ??
   285	          STRATEGY_INSTRUCTIONS.riskMetrics,
   286	        provenance:
   287	          rawCards.riskMetrics?.provenance ??
   288	          buildProvenance(generatedAt, tradeDate, "riskMetrics", trustedUrls),
   289	      },
   290	    };
   291	
   292	    const envelope: ApiEnvelope<StrategyPosture | null> = {
   293	      ok: true,
   294	      data: posture,
   295	      asOf: new Date().toISOString(),
   296	      source: ["analytics.market_posture", ...TRUSTED_MARKET_SOURCE_FEEDS].join(","),
   297	    };
   298	
   299	    return NextResponse.json({
   300	      ...envelope,
   301	      cards,
   302	      ai: toAiEnvelopeMeta(aiSnapshot),
   303	    });
   304	  } catch (err) {
   305	    return NextResponse.json(
   306	      { ok: false, data: null, asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: String(err) },
   307	      { status: 500 },
   308	    );
   309	  }
   310	}

   138	      "Provide monitoring cadence recommendation.",
   139	    ],
   140	  } satisfies StrategicSpecialInstructions,

   180	export async function GET() {
   181	  try {
   182	    const unauthorized = await requireAuthenticatedApiRequest();
   183	    if (unauthorized) {
   184	      return unauthorized;
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();
   188	    const aiSnapshot = await readAiSnapshot<SentimentAiSnapshot>(
   189	      "app/config/sentiment-overview-ai.json",
   190	    );
   191	    const trustedMarket = await fetchTrustedMarketSnapshot();
   192	    const trustedUrls = uniqueTrustedMarketUrls(trustedMarket);
   193	
   194	    const sevenDaysAgo = new Date();
   195	    sevenDaysAgo.setDate(sevenDaysAgo.getDate() - 7);
   196	    const oneDayAgo = new Date();
   197	    oneDayAgo.setDate(oneDayAgo.getDate() - 1);
   198	
   199	    const [{ data: newsRows, error: newsError }, { data: cftcRow }] = await Promise.all([
   200	      supabase
   201	        .schema("alt")
   202	        .from("news_events")
   203	        .select("source, published_at, specialist_tags")
   204	        .gte("published_at", sevenDaysAgo.toISOString())
   205	        .order("published_at", { ascending: false })
   206	        .limit(300),
   207	      supabase
   208	        .schema("mkt")
   209	        .from("cftc_1w")
   210	        .select("observation_date, payload")
   211	        .eq("symbol", "ZL")
   212	        .order("observation_date", { ascending: false })
   213	        .limit(1)
   214	        .maybeSingle(),
   215	    ]);
   216	
   217	    if (newsError) {
   218	      return NextResponse.json(
   219	        { ok: false, data: null, asOf: new Date().toISOString(), error: newsError.message },
   220	        { status: 500 },
   221	      );
   222	    }
   223	
   224	    const rows = newsRows ?? [];
   225	    const headlineCount = rows.length;
   226	    const last24h = rows.filter((row) => new Date(row.published_at).getTime() >= oneDayAgo.getTime()).length;
   227	    const pulseRatio = headlineCount > 0 ? last24h / Math.max(1, headlineCount / 7) : 0;
   228	    const flowState = pulseRatio >= 1.5 ? "elevated" : pulseRatio >= 1 ? "balanced" : "subdued";
   229	
   230	    const sourceSet = new Set<string>();
   231	    const tagCounts = new Map<string, number>();
   232	    for (const row of rows) {
   233	      if (row.source) sourceSet.add(row.source);
   234	      const tags = Array.isArray(row.specialist_tags) ? row.specialist_tags : [];
   235	      for (const tag of tags) {
   236	        const normalized = String(tag).trim();
   237	        if (!normalized) continue;
   238	        tagCounts.set(normalized, (tagCounts.get(normalized) ?? 0) + 1);
   239	      }
   240	    }
   241	    const topTags = Array.from(tagCounts.entries())
   242	      .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
   243	      .slice(0, 3)
   244	      .map(([tag]) => tag);
   245	    const tagPhrase = topTags.length > 0 ? topTags.join(", ") : "no dominant specialist cluster";
   246	
   247	    const cotPayload = cftcRow?.payload as Record<string, unknown> | null;
   248	    const cotBias = (cotPayload?.bias as string) ?? "neutral";
   249	    const cotBiasNorm = cotBias.trim().toLowerCase();
   250	    const cotBiasLabel =
   251	      cotBiasNorm.includes("bull") ? "bullish bias" : cotBiasNorm.includes("bear") ? "bearish bias" : "neutral bias";
   252	    const cotBiasScore = cotBiasNorm.includes("bull") ? 20 : cotBiasNorm.includes("bear") ? -20 : 0;
   253	
   254	    const vix = trustedMarket.vix.value;
   255	    const ovx = trustedMarket.ovx.value;
   256	    const cl5d = trustedMarket.cl.change5d;
   257	    const cl5dText =
   258	      cl5d === null ? "n/a" : `${cl5d * 100 >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${(cl5d * 100).toFixed(2)}%`;
   259	    const macroTrustedMissing = vix === null && ovx === null && cl5d === null;
   260	    const volatilityPenalty =
   261	      (vix !== null && vix >= 25 ? -14 : vix !== null && vix < 18 ? 6 : 0) +
   262	      (ovx !== null && ovx >= 35 ? -10 : ovx !== null && ovx < 26 ? 4 : 0) +
   263	      (cl5d !== null && Math.abs(cl5d) >= 0.04 ? -8 : cl5d !== null && Math.abs(cl5d) <= 0.015 ? 4 : 0);
   264	    const flowPenalty = pulseRatio >= 1.5 ? -12 : pulseRatio < 0.8 ? 5 : 0;
   265	    const sentimentScore = Math.max(-100, Math.min(100, cotBiasScore + volatilityPenalty + flowPenalty));
   266	
   267	    const dbOverview: SentimentOverview = {
   268	      headlineCount: headlineCount ?? 0,
   269	      sentimentScore,
   270	      cotBias,
   271	      updatedAt:
   272	        rows[0]?.published_at ??
   273	        (cftcRow?.observation_date ? `${cftcRow.observation_date}T00:00:00Z` : trustedMarket.fetchedAt),
   274	    };
   275	
   276	    const overview: SentimentOverview = {
   277	      headlineCount: aiSnapshot?.overview?.headlineCount ?? dbOverview.headlineCount,
   278	      sentimentScore: aiSnapshot?.overview?.sentimentScore ?? dbOverview.sentimentScore,
   279	      cotBias: aiSnapshot?.overview?.cotBias ?? dbOverview.cotBias,
   280	      updatedAt: aiSnapshot?.overview?.updatedAt ?? dbOverview.updatedAt,
   281	    };
   282	
   283	    const generatedAt = aiSnapshot?.generatedAt ?? new Date().toISOString();
   284	    const fallbackCards: SentimentCards = {
   285	      narratives: [
   286	        {
   287	          title: "Macro Narrative",
   288	          body: macroTrustedMissing
   289	            ? "Hard stop: trusted Yahoo/FRED market context is unavailable; macro narrative classification is blocked."
   290	            : `Macro pressure is ${sentimentScore <= -25 ? "defensive" : sentimentScore >= 25 ? "supportive" : "mixed"} with ${cotBiasLabel}. VIX ${vix?.toFixed(2) ?? "n/a"}, OVX ${ovx?.toFixed(2) ?? "n/a"}, and CL 5-day ${cl5dText} frame near-term narrative risk.`,
   291	          strategicSpecialInstructions: SENTIMENT_INSTRUCTIONS.macroNarrative,
   292	          provenance: buildProvenance(generatedAt, overview.updatedAt, "macroNarrative", trustedUrls),
   293	        },
   294	        {
   295	          title: "Flow Narrative",
   296	          body: headlineCount === 0
   297	            ? "Hard stop: no verified alt.news_events rows in the last 7 days; flow narrative is blocked."
   298	            : `Flow regime is ${flowState} with ${sourceSet.size} active sources and dominant specialist cluster: ${tagPhrase}. Velocity coherence is ${pulseRatio >= 1.5 ? "high-risk noisy" : pulseRatio >= 1 ? "tradable but mixed" : "low-intensity"} for buyer timing decisions.`,
   299	          strategicSpecialInstructions: SENTIMENT_INSTRUCTIONS.flowNarrative,
   300	          provenance: buildProvenance(generatedAt, overview.updatedAt, "flowNarrative", trustedUrls),
   301	        },
   302	        {
   303	          title: "Procurement Narrative",
   304	          body: macroTrustedMissing || !cftcRow
   305	            ? "Hard stop: missing verified CoT or trusted market context prevents buyer-facing procurement narrative."
   306	            : `Buyer pacing should remain ${sentimentScore <= -25 ? "defensive with tighter reassessment windows" : sentimentScore >= 25 ? "opportunistic staged accumulation" : "balanced with optionality preserved"}. CoT is ${cotBiasLabel} and volatility transmission remains ${vix !== null && vix >= 25 ? "elevated" : "contained"} at current read.`,
   307	          strategicSpecialInstructions: SENTIMENT_INSTRUCTIONS.procurementNarrative,
   308	          provenance: buildProvenance(generatedAt, overview.updatedAt, "procurementNarrative", trustedUrls),
   309	        },
   310	      ],
   311	      positioningFlow: {
   312	        title: "Managed Money Positioning",
   313	        body: !cftcRow
   314	          ? "Hard stop: no verified mkt.cftc_1w observation for ZL is available."
   315	          : `Latest CoT posture is ${cotBiasLabel} (observation ${cftcRow.observation_date}). Use this as directional conviction context, not a standalone execution trigger.`,
   316	        strategicSpecialInstructions: SENTIMENT_INSTRUCTIONS.positioningFlow,

    84	const AG_SOY_TAG_HINTS = new Set(["crush", "biofuel", "palm", "tariff", "china", "energy"]);
    85	
    86	function includesAnyTerm(text: string, terms: readonly string[]): boolean {
    87	  return terms.some((term) => {
    88	    const normalized = term.trim().toLowerCase();
    89	    if (!normalized) return false;
    90	    const escaped = normalized
    91	      .replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, "\\$&")
    92	      .replace(/\s+/g, "\\s+");
    93	    const pattern = new RegExp(`(^|[^a-z0-9])${escaped}([^a-z0-9]|$)`, "i");
    94	    return pattern.test(text);
    95	  });
    96	}
    97	
    98	function normalizeTags(raw: unknown): string[] {
    99	  if (!Array.isArray(raw)) return [];
   100	  return raw
   101	    .map((tag) => String(tag).trim())
   102	    .filter((tag) => tag.length > 0);
   103	}
   104	
   105	function isAgSoyPolicyRelevant(params: {
   106	  title: string;
   107	  summary?: string | null;
   108	  tags?: string[];
   109	}): boolean {
   110	  const textBlob = `${params.title} ${params.summary ?? ""}`.toLowerCase();
   111	  const primaryMatch = includesAnyTerm(textBlob, AG_SOY_PRIMARY_TERMS);
   112	  const contextMatch = includesAnyTerm(textBlob, AG_SOY_CONTEXT_TERMS);
   113	  const policyMatch = includesAnyTerm(textBlob, AG_SOY_POLICY_TERMS);
   114	  const tagSet = new Set((params.tags ?? []).map((tag) => tag.toLowerCase()));
   115	  const tagHint = Array.from(tagSet).some((tag) => AG_SOY_TAG_HINTS.has(tag));
   116	
   117	  if (primaryMatch) return true;
   118	  if (contextMatch && (policyMatch || tagHint)) return true;
   119	  if (tagHint && includesAnyTerm(textBlob, ["usda", "epa", "farm", "agricult", "renewable", "biofuel"])) {
   120	    return true;
   121	  }
   122	  return false;
   123	}
   124	
   125	function dedupeLegislationItems(items: LegislationItem[]): LegislationItem[] {
   126	  const seen = new Set<string>();
   127	  const deduped: LegislationItem[] = [];
   128	  for (const item of items) {
   129	    const key = `${item.source}::${item.title}`;
   130	    if (seen.has(key)) continue;
   131	    seen.add(key);
   132	    deduped.push(item);
   133	  }
   134	  return deduped;
   135	}

   254	  try {
   255	    const unauthorized = await requireAuthenticatedApiRequest();
   256	    if (unauthorized) {
   257	      return unauthorized;
   258	    }
   259	
   260	    const supabase = createSupabaseAdminClient();

   262	      "app/config/legislation-feed-ai.json",
   263	    );
   264	    const trustedMarket = await fetchTrustedMarketSnapshot();
   265	    const trustedUrls = uniqueTrustedMarketUrls(trustedMarket);
   266	
   267	    const [legRes, execRes, billsRes] = await Promise.all([
   268	      supabase
   269	        .schema("alt")
   270	        .from("legislation_1d")
   271	        .select("title, summary, source, published_at, payload")
   272	        .order("published_at", { ascending: false })
   273	        .limit(20),
   274	      supabase
   275	        .schema("alt")
   276	        .from("executive_actions")
   277	        .select("title, summary, source, published_at, payload")
   278	        .order("published_at", { ascending: false })
   279	        .limit(10),
   280	      supabase
   281	        .schema("alt")
   282	        .from("congress_bills")
   283	        .select("title, summary, source, published_at, payload")
   284	        .order("published_at", { ascending: false })
   285	        .limit(10),
   286	    ]);
   287	
   288	    const allRows = [...(legRes.data ?? []), ...(execRes.data ?? []), ...(billsRes.data ?? [])];
   289	    allRows.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.published_at).getTime() - new Date(a.published_at).getTime());
   290	
   291	    const filteredRows = allRows.filter((row) => {
   292	      const payload = (row.payload as Record<string, unknown> | null) ?? null;
   293	      const tags = normalizeTags(payload?.tags);
   294	      return isAgSoyPolicyRelevant({
   295	        title: String(row.title ?? ""),
   296	        summary: row.summary as string | null | undefined,
   297	        tags,
   298	      });
   299	    });
   300	
   301	    const dbItems = dedupeLegislationItems(filteredRows.slice(0, 30).map((row) => {
   302	      const payload = (row.payload as Record<string, unknown> | null) ?? null;
   303	      return {
   304	        source: row.source,
   305	        title: row.title,
   306	        publishedAt: row.published_at,
   307	        tags: normalizeTags(payload?.tags),
   308	      };
   309	    }));
   310	
   311	    const snapshotItems = dedupeLegislationItems((aiSnapshot?.items ?? []).filter((item) =>
   312	      isAgSoyPolicyRelevant({
   313	        title: item.title,
   314	        summary: "",
   315	        tags: item.tags ?? [],
   316	      }),
   317	    ));
   318	    const items: LegislationItem[] = dbItems.length > 0 ? dbItems : snapshotItems;
   319	    const generatedAt = aiSnapshot?.generatedAt ?? new Date().toISOString();
   320	    const asOf = items[0]?.publishedAt ?? trustedMarket.fetchedAt;
   321	
   322	    const sourceCounts = new Map<string, number>();
   323	    const tagCounts = new Map<string, number>();
   324	    for (const item of dbItems) {
   325	      sourceCounts.set(item.source, (sourceCounts.get(item.source) ?? 0) + 1);
   326	      for (const tag of item.tags) {
   327	        const normalized = String(tag).trim();
   328	        if (!normalized) continue;
   329	        tagCounts.set(normalized, (tagCounts.get(normalized) ?? 0) + 1);
   330	      }
   331	    }
   332	    const sortedSources = Array.from(sourceCounts.entries()).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
   333	    const sortedTags = Array.from(tagCounts.entries()).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
   334	    const topSource = sortedSources[0];
   335	    const topTagSet = sortedTags.slice(0, 3).map(([tag]) => tag).join(", ");
   336	    const topSourceShare =
   337	      dbItems.length > 0 && topSource ? (topSource[1] / dbItems.length) * 100 : null;
   338	    const concentrationClass =
   339	      topSourceShare === null

    45	function toDateIso(ts: number | null | undefined): string | null {
    46	  if (typeof ts !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(ts)) return null;
    47	  return new Date(ts * 1000).toISOString();
    48	}

    50	async function fetchJson<T>(url: string): Promise<T | null> {
    51	  try {
    52	    const res = await fetch(url, {
    53	      headers: {
    54	        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Codex Trusted Source Pull)",
    55	      },
    56	      cache: "no-store",
    57	    });
    58	    if (!res.ok) return null;
    59	    return (await res.json()) as T;
    60	  } catch {
    61	    return null;
    62	  }
    63	}

    65	async function fetchYahooSeries(symbol: string): Promise<TrustedSeriesPoint & { change5d: number | null }> {
    66	  const url = `https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(
    67	    symbol,
    68	  )}?interval=1d&range=1mo`;
    69	  const payload = await fetchJson<YahooChartResponse>(url);
    70	  const result = payload?.chart?.result?.[0];
    71	  const timestamps = result?.timestamp ?? [];
    72	  const closes = result?.indicators?.quote?.[0]?.close ?? [];
    73	
    74	  let latestClose: number | null = null;
    75	  let latestTs: number | null = null;
    76	  for (let i = closes.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
    77	    const close = closes[i];
    78	    if (typeof close === "number" && Number.isFinite(close)) {
    79	      latestClose = close;
    80	      latestTs = timestamps[i] ?? null;
    81	      break;
    82	    }
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  let anchorClose: number | null = null;
    86	  let validSeen = 0;
    87	  for (let i = closes.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
    88	    const close = closes[i];
    89	    if (typeof close !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(close)) continue;
    90	    validSeen += 1;
    91	    if (validSeen >= 6) {
    92	      anchorClose = close;
    93	      break;
    94	    }
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  const change5d =
    98	    latestClose !== null && anchorClose !== null && anchorClose !== 0
    99	      ? (latestClose - anchorClose) / anchorClose
   100	      : null;
   101	
   102	  return {
   103	    value: latestClose,
   104	    asOf: toDateIso(latestTs ?? result?.meta?.regularMarketTime ?? null),
   105	    source: "Yahoo Finance",
   106	    url,
   107	    change5d,
   108	  };
   109	}
   110	
   111	async function fetchFredLatest(seriesId: string): Promise<TrustedSeriesPoint> {
   112	  const url = `https://fred.stlouisfed.org/graph/fredgraph.csv?id=${encodeURIComponent(seriesId)}`;
   113	  try {
   114	    const res = await fetch(url, { cache: "no-store" });
   115	    if (!res.ok) {
   116	      return { value: null, asOf: null, source: "FRED", url };
   117	    }
   118	    const csv = await res.text();
   119	    const lines = csv.trim().split("\n");
   120	    for (let i = lines.length - 1; i >= 1; i -= 1) {
   121	      const row = lines[i];
   122	      const [date, value] = row.split(",", 2);
   123	      if (!date || !value || value === ".") continue;
   124	      const n = Number(value);
   125	      if (!Number.isFinite(n)) continue;
   126	      return {
   127	        value: n,
   128	        asOf: new Date(`${date}T00:00:00Z`).toISOString(),
   129	        source: "FRED",
   130	        url,
   131	      };
   132	    }
   133	  } catch {
   134	    return { value: null, asOf: null, source: "FRED", url };
   135	  }
   136	  return { value: null, asOf: null, source: "FRED", url };
   137	}
   138	
   139	export async function fetchTrustedMarketSnapshot(): Promise<TrustedMarketSnapshot> {
   140	  const [zl, cl, cny, vix, ovx] = await Promise.all([
   141	    fetchYahooSeries("ZL=F"),
   142	    fetchYahooSeries("CL=F"),
   143	    fetchYahooSeries("CNY=X"),
   144	    fetchFredLatest("VIXCLS"),
   145	    fetchFredLatest("OVXCLS"),
   146	  ]);
   147	
   148	  return {
   149	    fetchedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   150	    zl,
   151	    cl,
   152	    cny,
   153	    vix,
   154	    ovx,
   155	  };
   156	}

   158	export function uniqueTrustedMarketUrls(snapshot: TrustedMarketSnapshot): string[] {
   159	  return [snapshot.zl.url, snapshot.cl.url, snapshot.cny.url, snapshot.vix.url, snapshot.ovx.url]
   160	    .filter((u, idx, arr) => typeof u === "string" && arr.indexOf(u) === idx);
   161	}

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql | sed -n '1,260p'" in /Users/zincdigital/mnt/SatechiHub/ZINC-FUSION-V16
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	-- =============================================================================
     2	-- ingest_zl_intraday() + rollup_zl_daily()
     3	--
     4	-- Pulls 1h ZL bars from Databento REST API into mkt.price_1h.
     5	-- Rolls up 1h bars into mkt.price_1d daily bars.
     6	-- Updates mkt.latest_price with the most recent close.
     7	-- Logs all runs to ops.ingest_run.
     8	--
     9	-- pg_cron: runs hourly. 1h bars form the daily bar progressively.
    10	-- =============================================================================
    11	
    12	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    13	-- Function A: ingest_zl_intraday()
    14	--
    15	-- Fetches 1h OHLCV bars from Databento for ZL continuous front-month.
    16	-- Uses the newest bar in mkt.price_1h to determine the start date.
    17	-- Databento returns NDJSON (newline-delimited JSON lines).
    18	-- Prices are fixed-point integers (divide by 1e9).
    19	-- ts_event is nanosecond epoch.
    20	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    21	CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION ingest_zl_intraday()
    22	RETURNS jsonb
    23	SECURITY DEFINER
    24	SET search_path = public, extensions
    25	LANGUAGE plpgsql
    26	AS $$
    27	DECLARE
    28	  api_key     TEXT;
    29	  start_date  TEXT;
    30	  end_date    TEXT;
    31	  url         TEXT;
    32	  response    http_response;
    33	  line        TEXT;
    34	  rec         JSONB;
    35	  bar_ts      TIMESTAMPTZ;
    36	  bar_open    NUMERIC;
    37	  bar_high    NUMERIC;
    38	  bar_low     NUMERIC;
    39	  bar_close   NUMERIC;
    40	  bar_volume  BIGINT;
    41	  records_in  INT := 0;
    42	  started     TIMESTAMPTZ := now();
    43	BEGIN
    44	  -- 1. Get API key from Vault
    45	  SELECT decrypted_secret INTO api_key
    46	  FROM vault.decrypted_secrets
    47	  WHERE name = 'databento_api_key_v2';
    48	
    49	  IF api_key IS NULL THEN
    50	    INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
    51	    VALUES ('ingest_zl_intraday', 'databento', started, now(), 'failed', 0, 'Databento API key not found in Vault');
    52	    RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'error', 'message', 'API key not in Vault');
    53	  END IF;
    54	
    55	  -- 2. Determine date range: start from max existing 1h bar or 30 days back
    56	  SELECT COALESCE(
    57	    to_char((max(bucket_ts) AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD'),
    58	    to_char((now() - interval '30 days')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD')
    59	  ) INTO start_date
    60	  FROM mkt.price_1h
    61	  WHERE symbol = 'ZL';
    62	
    63	  -- End = today (Databento will clamp to available data)
    64	  end_date := to_char((now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    65	
    66	  -- If start = end, go back 1 day to ensure we get today's bars
    67	  IF start_date = end_date THEN
    68	    start_date := to_char(((now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC') - interval '1 day')::date, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    69	  END IF;
    70	
    71	  -- 3. Call Databento REST API
    72	  url := 'https://hist.databento.com/v0/timeseries.get_range'
    73	    || '?dataset=GLBX.MDP3'
    74	    || '&symbols=ZL.c.0'
    75	    || '&schema=ohlcv-1h'
    76	    || '&stype_in=continuous'
    77	    || '&start=' || start_date
    78	    || '&end=' || end_date
    79	    || '&encoding=json';
    80	
    81	  SELECT * INTO response FROM http((
    82	    'GET',
    83	    url,
    84	    ARRAY[http_header('Authorization', 'Basic ' || encode(convert_to(api_key || ':', 'UTF8'), 'base64'))],
    85	    NULL,
    86	    NULL
    87	  )::http_request);
    88	
    89	  IF response.status != 200 THEN
    90	    INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
    91	    VALUES ('ingest_zl_intraday', 'databento', started, now(), 'failed', 0,
    92	            'Databento HTTP ' || response.status || ': ' || left(response.content, 200));
    93	    RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'error', 'http_status', response.status);
    94	  END IF;
    95	
    96	  -- 4. Parse NDJSON response (one JSON object per line)
    97	  FOR line IN SELECT unnest(string_to_array(response.content, E'\n'))
    98	  LOOP
    99	    -- Skip empty lines
   100	    CONTINUE WHEN trim(line) = '';
   101	
   102	    BEGIN
   103	      rec := line::jsonb;
   104	
   105	      -- ts_event is nanosecond epoch -> convert to timestamptz
   106	      bar_ts := to_timestamp(((rec->'hd'->>'ts_event')::bigint) / 1000000000.0);
   107	
   108	      -- Prices are fixed-point (divide by 1e9)
   109	      bar_open   := (rec->>'open')::bigint   / 1000000000.0;
   110	      bar_high   := (rec->>'high')::bigint   / 1000000000.0;
   111	      bar_low    := (rec->>'low')::bigint    / 1000000000.0;
   112	      bar_close  := (rec->>'close')::bigint  / 1000000000.0;
   113	      bar_volume := (rec->>'volume')::bigint;
   114	
   115	      -- Skip bars with zero or null close
   116	      CONTINUE WHEN bar_close IS NULL OR bar_close = 0;
   117	
   118	      -- UPSERT into mkt.price_1h
   119	      INSERT INTO mkt.price_1h (symbol, bucket_ts, open, high, low, close, volume)
   120	      VALUES ('ZL', bar_ts, bar_open, bar_high, bar_low, bar_close, bar_volume)
   121	      ON CONFLICT (symbol, bucket_ts) DO UPDATE SET
   122	        open       = EXCLUDED.open,
   123	        high       = EXCLUDED.high,
   124	        low        = EXCLUDED.low,
   125	        close      = EXCLUDED.close,
   126	        volume     = EXCLUDED.volume,
   127	        ingested_at = now();
   128	
   129	      records_in := records_in + 1;
   130	
   131	    EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
   132	      -- Skip malformed lines, continue processing
   133	      CONTINUE;
   134	    END;
   135	  END LOOP;
   136	
   137	  -- 5. Log success
   138	  INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
   139	  VALUES ('ingest_zl_intraday', 'databento', started, now(), 'ok', records_in, NULL);
   140	
   141	  RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'ok', 'records', records_in, 'start', start_date, 'end', end_date);
   142	END;
   143	$$;
   144	
   145	
   146	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   147	-- Function B: rollup_zl_daily()
   148	--
   149	-- Aggregates 1h bars from mkt.price_1h into mkt.price_1d.
   150	-- For each calendar day with 1h bars:
   151	--   open  = open of first 1h bar (by bucket_ts)
   152	--   high  = max high across all 1h bars
   153	--   low   = min low across all 1h bars
   154	--   close = close of last 1h bar (by bucket_ts)
   155	--   volume = sum of all 1h bar volumes
   156	--
   157	-- Also updates mkt.latest_price with the most recent close.
   158	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   159	CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION rollup_zl_daily()
   160	RETURNS jsonb
   161	SECURITY DEFINER
   162	SET search_path = public
   163	LANGUAGE plpgsql
   164	AS $$
   165	DECLARE
   166	  records_out INT := 0;
   167	  started     TIMESTAMPTZ := now();
   168	  latest_close NUMERIC;
   169	  latest_ts    TIMESTAMPTZ;
   170	BEGIN
   171	  -- 1. Aggregate 1h bars into daily bars
   172	  --    Only process days that have 1h bars newer than the latest ingested_at in price_1d,
   173	  --    OR days that don't exist in price_1d yet.
   174	  INSERT INTO mkt.price_1d (symbol, bucket_ts, open, high, low, close, volume)
   175	  SELECT
   176	    'ZL' AS symbol,
   177	    date_trunc('day', bucket_ts AT TIME ZONE 'UTC') AS day_ts,
   178	    (ARRAY_AGG(open ORDER BY bucket_ts ASC))[1]  AS open,
   179	    MAX(high)                                      AS high,
   180	    MIN(low)                                       AS low,
   181	    (ARRAY_AGG(close ORDER BY bucket_ts DESC))[1] AS close,
   182	    SUM(volume)                                    AS volume
   183	  FROM mkt.price_1h
   184	  WHERE symbol = 'ZL'
   185	    AND bucket_ts >= COALESCE(
   186	      (SELECT max(bucket_ts) - interval '2 days' FROM mkt.price_1d WHERE symbol = 'ZL'),
   187	      '2020-01-01'::timestamptz
   188	    )
   189	  GROUP BY date_trunc('day', bucket_ts AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')
   190	  HAVING SUM(volume) >= 100  -- skip roll artifact days (< 100 total contracts)
   191	  ON CONFLICT (symbol, bucket_ts) DO UPDATE SET
   192	    open       = EXCLUDED.open,
   193	    high       = EXCLUDED.high,
   194	    low        = EXCLUDED.low,
   195	    close      = EXCLUDED.close,
   196	    volume     = EXCLUDED.volume,
   197	    ingested_at = now();
   198	
   199	  GET DIAGNOSTICS records_out = ROW_COUNT;
   200	
   201	  -- 2. Update latest_price with most recent close
   202	  SELECT close, bucket_ts INTO latest_close, latest_ts
   203	  FROM mkt.price_1d
   204	  WHERE symbol = 'ZL'
   205	  ORDER BY bucket_ts DESC
   206	  LIMIT 1;
   207	
   208	  IF latest_close IS NOT NULL THEN
   209	    INSERT INTO mkt.latest_price (symbol, price, observed_at, ingested_at)
   210	    VALUES ('ZL', latest_close, latest_ts, now())
   211	    ON CONFLICT (symbol) DO UPDATE SET
   212	      price       = EXCLUDED.price,
   213	      observed_at = EXCLUDED.observed_at,
   214	      ingested_at = now();
   215	  END IF;
   216	
   217	  -- 3. Log success
   218	  INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (job_name, source, started_at, finished_at, status, records_upserted, error_message)
   219	  VALUES ('rollup_zl_daily', 'rollup', started, now(), 'ok', records_out, NULL);
   220	
   221	  RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'ok', 'daily_bars_upserted', records_out, 'latest_price', latest_close);
   222	END;
   223	$$;
   224	
   225	
   226	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   227	-- pg_cron schedules: hourly, staggered off :00
   228	-- ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   229	SELECT cron.schedule('ingest_zl_intraday', '7 * * * *', $$SELECT ingest_zl_intraday()$$);
   230	SELECT cron.schedule('rollup_zl_daily',    '9 * * * *', $$SELECT rollup_zl_daily()$$);
