 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	-- Supabase-only trusted dashboard fill:
     2	-- refreshes analytics risk-factor metrics/attribution from live market pulls
     3	-- and carries forward non-market fields until AG training publishes fresh rows.
     4	
     5	CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill()
     6	RETURNS jsonb
     7	SECURITY DEFINER
     8	SET search_path = public, extensions
     9	LANGUAGE plpgsql
    10	AS $$
    11	DECLARE
    12	  v_run_id UUID := gen_random_uuid();
    13	  started TIMESTAMPTZ := now();
    14	  v_trade_date DATE := (now() AT TIME ZONE 'America/New_York')::date;
    15	  now_et_iso TEXT := to_char(now() AT TIME ZONE 'America/New_York', 'YYYY-MM-DD"T"HH24:MI:SSOF');
    16	  prev_date DATE;
    17	
    18	  resp_cl http_response;
    19	  resp_cny http_response;
    20	  resp_vix http_response;
    21	  resp_ovx http_response;
    22	
    23	  cl_price NUMERIC;
    24	  cl_anchor NUMERIC;
    25	  cl_change_5d NUMERIC;
    26	  cny_rate NUMERIC;
    27	  vix_value NUMERIC;
    28	  ovx_value NUMERIC;
    29	
    30	  board_crush_value NUMERIC;
    31	  oil_share_value NUMERIC;
    32	  oil_share_5d_change NUMERIC;
    33	  uncertainty_value NUMERIC;
    34	  soy_china_news_count NUMERIC;
    35	  soy_tariff_news_count NUMERIC;
    36	  macro_news_count NUMERIC;
    37	  energy_news_count NUMERIC;
    38	
    39	  vix_stress_score NUMERIC;
    40	  crush_pressure_score NUMERIC;
    41	  china_tension_score NUMERIC;
    42	  tariff_threat_score NUMERIC;
    43	  energy_stress_score NUMERIC;
    44	
    45	  avg_score NUMERIC;
    46	  top_driver_key TEXT;
    47	  top_driver_score NUMERIC;
    48	  posture TEXT;
    49	  regime TEXT;
    50	  regime_confidence NUMERIC;
    51	  v_records_upserted INT := 0;
    52	  non_null_points INT := 0;
    53	  payload JSONB;
    54	BEGIN
    55	  INSERT INTO ops.ingest_run (run_id, job_name, source, status, started_at)
    56	  VALUES (v_run_id, 'trusted_site_fill', 'supabase-http-yahoo', 'running', started);
    57	
    58	  -- Avoid transient HTTP timeout failures in pgsql-http.
    59	  PERFORM extensions.http_set_curlopt('CURLOPT_CONNECTTIMEOUT_MS', '5000');
    60	  PERFORM extensions.http_set_curlopt('CURLOPT_TIMEOUT_MS', '20000');
    61	
    62	  SELECT max(trade_date) INTO prev_date
    63	  FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    64	  WHERE trade_date <= v_trade_date;
    65	
    66	  IF prev_date IS NOT NULL THEN
    67	    SELECT metric_value INTO board_crush_value
    68	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    69	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'board_crush_value'
    70	    LIMIT 1;
    71	
    72	    SELECT metric_value INTO oil_share_value
    73	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    74	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'oil_share_value'
    75	    LIMIT 1;
    76	
    77	    SELECT metric_value INTO oil_share_5d_change
    78	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    79	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'oil_share_5d_change'
    80	    LIMIT 1;
    81	
    82	    SELECT metric_value INTO uncertainty_value
    83	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    84	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'uncertainty_value'
    85	    LIMIT 1;
    86	
    87	    SELECT metric_value INTO soy_china_news_count
    88	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    89	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'soy_china_news_count'
    90	    LIMIT 1;
    91	
    92	    SELECT metric_value INTO soy_tariff_news_count
    93	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    94	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'soy_tariff_news_count'
    95	    LIMIT 1;
    96	
    97	    SELECT metric_value INTO macro_news_count
    98	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
    99	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'macro_news_count'
   100	    LIMIT 1;
   101	
   102	    SELECT metric_value INTO energy_news_count
   103	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   104	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'energy_news_count'
   105	    LIMIT 1;
   106	  END IF;
   107	
   108	  SELECT * INTO resp_cl
   109	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/CL%3DF?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   110	  IF resp_cl.status = 200 THEN
   111	    WITH closes AS (
   112	      SELECT ordinality AS idx, value::text::numeric AS close
   113	      FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   114	        COALESCE(resp_cl.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   115	      ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   116	      WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   117	    ),
   118	    latest AS (
   119	      SELECT idx, close FROM closes ORDER BY idx DESC LIMIT 1
   120	    ),
   121	    anchor AS (
   122	      SELECT close FROM closes WHERE idx <= (SELECT idx FROM latest) - 5 ORDER BY idx DESC LIMIT 1
   123	    )
   124	    SELECT l.close, a.close
   125	      INTO cl_price, cl_anchor
   126	    FROM latest l
   127	    LEFT JOIN anchor a ON TRUE;
   128	  END IF;
   129	  IF cl_anchor IS NOT NULL AND cl_anchor <> 0 THEN
   130	    cl_change_5d := (cl_price - cl_anchor) / cl_anchor;
   131	  END IF;
   132	
   133	  SELECT * INTO resp_cny
   134	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/CNY%3DX?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   135	  IF resp_cny.status = 200 THEN
   136	    SELECT value::text::numeric INTO cny_rate
   137	    FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   138	      COALESCE(resp_cny.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   139	    ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   140	    WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   141	    ORDER BY ordinality DESC
   142	    LIMIT 1;
   143	  END IF;
   144	
   145	  SELECT * INTO resp_vix
   146	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/%5EVIX?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   147	  IF resp_vix.status = 200 THEN
   148	    SELECT value::text::numeric INTO vix_value
   149	    FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   150	      COALESCE(resp_vix.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   151	    ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   152	    WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   153	    ORDER BY ordinality DESC
   154	    LIMIT 1;
   155	  END IF;
   156	
   157	  SELECT * INTO resp_ovx
   158	  FROM extensions.http_get('https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/%5EOVX?interval=1d&range=1mo');
   159	  IF resp_ovx.status = 200 THEN
   160	    SELECT value::text::numeric INTO ovx_value
   161	    FROM jsonb_array_elements(
   162	      COALESCE(resp_ovx.content::jsonb #> '{chart,result,0,indicators,quote,0,close}', '[]'::jsonb)
   163	    ) WITH ORDINALITY AS e(value, ordinality)
   164	    WHERE jsonb_typeof(value) = 'number'
   165	    ORDER BY ordinality DESC
   166	    LIMIT 1;
   167	  END IF;
   168	
   169	  -- If live pulls fail, keep last known values so the surface does not hard-break.
   170	  IF cl_price IS NULL THEN
   171	    SELECT metric_value INTO cl_price
   172	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   173	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'cl_price'
   174	    LIMIT 1;
   175	  END IF;
   176	  IF cl_change_5d IS NULL THEN
   177	    SELECT metric_value INTO cl_change_5d
   178	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   179	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'cl_change_5d'
   180	    LIMIT 1;
   181	  END IF;
   182	  IF cny_rate IS NULL THEN
   183	    SELECT metric_value INTO cny_rate
   184	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   185	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'cny_rate'
   186	    LIMIT 1;
   187	  END IF;
   188	  IF vix_value IS NULL THEN
   189	    SELECT metric_value INTO vix_value
   190	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   191	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'vix_value'
   192	    LIMIT 1;
   193	  END IF;
   194	  IF ovx_value IS NULL THEN
   195	    SELECT metric_value INTO ovx_value
   196	    FROM analytics.dashboard_metrics
   197	    WHERE trade_date = prev_date AND metric_key = 'ovx_value'
   198	    LIMIT 1;
   199	  END IF;
   200	
   201	  soy_china_news_count := COALESCE(soy_china_news_count, 0);
   202	  soy_tariff_news_count := COALESCE(soy_tariff_news_count, 0);
   203	  macro_news_count := COALESCE(macro_news_count, 0);
   204	  energy_news_count := COALESCE(energy_news_count, 0);
   205	
   206	  vix_stress_score := round((
   207	    (CASE WHEN vix_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((vix_value - 14) / 21) * 100)) END) * 0.60 +
   208	    (CASE WHEN ovx_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((ovx_value - 25) / 55) * 100)) END) * 0.40
   209	  )::numeric, 1);
   210	
   211	  crush_pressure_score := round((
   212	    (CASE WHEN board_crush_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, (((4.2 - board_crush_value) - 0.0) / 3.5) * 100)) END) * 0.70 +
   213	    (CASE WHEN oil_share_5d_change IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((abs(oil_share_5d_change) - 0.2) / 3.8) * 100)) END) * 0.30
   214	  )::numeric, 1);
   215	
   216	  china_tension_score := round((
   217	    (CASE WHEN cny_rate IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((abs(cny_rate - 7.0) - 0.02) / 0.33) * 100)) END) * 0.70 +
   218	    (GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((soy_china_news_count - 2) / 28) * 100))) * 0.30
   219	  )::numeric, 1);
   220	
   221	  tariff_threat_score := round((
   222	    (CASE WHEN uncertainty_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((uncertainty_value - 150) / 400) * 100)) END) * 0.70 +
   223	    (GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, (((soy_tariff_news_count + macro_news_count) - 4) / 36) * 100))) * 0.30
   224	  )::numeric, 1);
   225	
   226	  energy_stress_score := round((
   227	    (CASE WHEN cl_change_5d IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, (((abs(cl_change_5d * 100)) - 0.8) / 9.2) * 100)) END) * 0.55 +
   228	    (CASE WHEN ovx_value IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((ovx_value - 25) / 55) * 100)) END) * 0.30 +
   229	    (GREATEST(0, LEAST(100, ((energy_news_count - 2) / 28) * 100))) * 0.15
   230	  )::numeric, 1);
   231	
   232	  avg_score := round(((vix_stress_score + crush_pressure_score + china_tension_score + tariff_threat_score + energy_stress_score) / 5.0)::numeric, 1);
   233	
   234	  top_driver_key := 'vix_stress';
   235	  top_driver_score := vix_stress_score;
   236	  IF crush_pressure_score > top_driver_score THEN
   237	    top_driver_key := 'crush_pressure';
   238	    top_driver_score := crush_pressure_score;
   239	  END IF;
   240	  IF china_tension_score > top_driver_score THEN
   241	    top_driver_key := 'china_tension';
   242	    top_driver_score := china_tension_score;
   243	  END IF;
   244	  IF tariff_threat_score > top_driver_score THEN
   245	    top_driver_key := 'tariff_threat';
   246	    top_driver_score := tariff_threat_score;
   247	  END IF;
   248	  IF energy_stress_score > top_driver_score THEN
   249	    top_driver_key := 'energy_stress';
   250	    top_driver_score := energy_stress_score;
   251	  END IF;
   252	
   253	  IF avg_score >= 78 AND top_driver_score >= 85 THEN
   254	    posture := 'DEFER';
   255	  ELSIF avg_score >= 62 THEN
   256	    posture := 'WAIT';
   257	  ELSE
   258	    posture := 'ACCUMULATE';
   259	  END IF;
   260	
   261	  IF avg_score >= 70 THEN
   262	    regime := 'SUPPLY_CRISIS';
   263	  ELSIF avg_score >= 55 THEN
   264	    regime := 'BEARISH';
   265	  ELSIF avg_score <= 30 THEN
   266	    regime := 'BULLISH';
   267	  ELSE
   268	    regime := 'NEUTRAL';
   269	  END IF;
   270	
   271	  non_null_points :=
   272	    (CASE WHEN cl_price IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   273	    (CASE WHEN cl_change_5d IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   274	    (CASE WHEN cny_rate IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   275	    (CASE WHEN vix_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   276	    (CASE WHEN ovx_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   277	    (CASE WHEN board_crush_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   278	    (CASE WHEN oil_share_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   279	    (CASE WHEN oil_share_5d_change IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) +
   280	    (CASE WHEN uncertainty_value IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END);
   281	  regime_confidence := round(LEAST(0.95, 0.45 + non_null_points * 0.05)::numeric, 4);
   282	
   283	  payload := jsonb_build_object(
   284	    'source', 'supabase_pg_cron_trusted_fill',
   285	    'asOf', now_et_iso,
   286	    'carriedFromDate', prev_date,
   287	    'pulledBy', 'ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill'
   288	  );
   289	
   290	  INSERT INTO analytics.dashboard_metrics (trade_date, metric_key, metric_value, payload)
   291	  VALUES
   292	    (v_trade_date, 'vix_value', vix_value, payload),
   293	    (v_trade_date, 'ovx_value', ovx_value, payload),
   294	    (v_trade_date, 'cl_price', cl_price, payload),
   295	    (v_trade_date, 'cl_change_5d', cl_change_5d, payload),
   296	    (v_trade_date, 'oil_change_5d', cl_change_5d, payload),
   297	    (v_trade_date, 'cny_rate', cny_rate, payload),
   298	    (v_trade_date, 'board_crush_value', board_crush_value, payload),
   299	    (v_trade_date, 'oil_share_value', oil_share_value, payload),
   300	    (v_trade_date, 'oil_share_5d_change', oil_share_5d_change, payload),
   301	    (v_trade_date, 'uncertainty_value', uncertainty_value, payload),
   302	    (v_trade_date, 'tpu_value', uncertainty_value, payload),
   303	    (v_trade_date, 'soy_china_news_count', soy_china_news_count, payload),
   304	    (v_trade_date, 'soy_tariff_news_count', soy_tariff_news_count, payload),
   305	    (v_trade_date, 'macro_news_count', macro_news_count, payload),
   306	    (v_trade_date, 'energy_news_count', energy_news_count, payload),
   307	    (v_trade_date, 'vix_stress_score', vix_stress_score, payload),
   308	    (v_trade_date, 'crush_pressure_score', crush_pressure_score, payload),
   309	    (v_trade_date, 'china_tension_score', china_tension_score, payload),
   310	    (v_trade_date, 'tariff_threat_score', tariff_threat_score, payload),
   311	    (v_trade_date, 'energy_stress_score', energy_stress_score, payload)
   312	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date, metric_key) DO UPDATE
   313	    SET metric_value = EXCLUDED.metric_value,
   314	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   315	        ingested_at = now();
   316	  GET DIAGNOSTICS v_records_upserted = ROW_COUNT;
   317	
   318	  INSERT INTO analytics.driver_attribution_1d (trade_date, rank, factor, contribution, confidence, payload)
   319	  VALUES
   320	    (v_trade_date, 1, 'energy_transmission', energy_stress_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(energy_stress_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   321	    (v_trade_date, 2, 'macro_policy_uncertainty', tariff_threat_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(tariff_threat_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   322	    (v_trade_date, 3, 'china_flow_currency', china_tension_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(china_tension_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   323	    (v_trade_date, 4, 'crush_margin_oil_share', crush_pressure_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(crush_pressure_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload),
   324	    (v_trade_date, 5, 'vix_volatility_regime', vix_stress_score, round(LEAST(0.95, 0.5 + abs(vix_stress_score - 50.0) / 120.0)::numeric, 4), payload)
   325	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date, rank) DO UPDATE
   326	    SET factor = EXCLUDED.factor,
   327	        contribution = EXCLUDED.contribution,
   328	        confidence = EXCLUDED.confidence,
   329	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   330	        ingested_at = now();
   331	
   332	  INSERT INTO analytics.market_posture (trade_date, posture, rationale, payload)
   333	  VALUES (
   334	    v_trade_date,
   335	    posture,
   336	    format(
   337	      'Buyer posture %s from average score %s; top channel %s at %s.',
   338	      posture,
   339	      to_char(avg_score, 'FM999990.0'),
   340	      top_driver_key,
   341	      to_char(top_driver_score, 'FM999990.0')
   342	    ),
   343	    jsonb_build_object('averageScore', avg_score, 'topDriver', top_driver_key, 'topDriverScore', top_driver_score, 'asOf', now_et_iso, 'source', 'supabase_pg_cron_trusted_fill')
   344	  )
   345	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date) DO UPDATE
   346	    SET posture = EXCLUDED.posture,
   347	        rationale = EXCLUDED.rationale,
   348	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   349	        ingested_at = now();
   350	
   351	  INSERT INTO analytics.regime_state_1d (trade_date, regime, confidence, payload)
   352	  VALUES (
   353	    v_trade_date,
   354	    regime,
   355	    regime_confidence,
   356	    jsonb_build_object('averageScore', avg_score, 'asOf', now_et_iso, 'source', 'supabase_pg_cron_trusted_fill')
   357	  )
   358	  ON CONFLICT (trade_date) DO UPDATE
   359	    SET regime = EXCLUDED.regime,
   360	        confidence = EXCLUDED.confidence,
   361	        payload = EXCLUDED.payload,
   362	        ingested_at = now();
   363	
   364	  UPDATE ops.ingest_run
   365	  SET status = 'ok',
   366	      finished_at = now(),
   367	      records_upserted = v_records_upserted,
   368	      error_message = NULL,
   369	      ingested_at = now()
   370	  WHERE run_id = v_run_id;
   371	
   372	  RETURN jsonb_build_object(
   373	    'status', 'ok',
   374	    'tradeDate', v_trade_date,
   375	    'recordsUpserted', v_records_upserted,
   376	    'topDriver', top_driver_key,
   377	    'topScore', top_driver_score,
   378	    'averageScore', avg_score
   379	  );
   380	EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
   381	  UPDATE ops.ingest_run
   382	  SET status = 'error',
   383	      finished_at = now(),
   384	      error_message = left(SQLERRM, 1000),
   385	      ingested_at = now()
   386	  WHERE run_id = v_run_id;
   387	  RETURN jsonb_build_object('status', 'error', 'message', SQLERRM);
   388	END;
   389	$$;
   390	
   391	DO $$
   392	DECLARE
   393	  job_id BIGINT;
   394	BEGIN
   395	  FOR job_id IN
   396	    SELECT jobid
   397	    FROM cron.job
   398	    WHERE jobname = 'trusted_site_fill'
   399	       OR command ILIKE '%ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill(%'
   400	  LOOP
   401	    PERFORM cron.unschedule(job_id);
   402	  END LOOP;
   403	END
   404	$$;
   405	
   406	-- Hourly refresh at :17 to keep dashboard drivers fresh without high-frequency pull cost.
   407	SELECT cron.schedule(
   408	  'trusted_site_fill',
   409	  '17 * * * *',
   410	  $$SELECT ops.ingest_trusted_site_fill()$$
   411	);

    19	
    20	## Features
    21	
    22	- Works across the entire [Next.js](https://nextjs.org) stack
    23	  - App Router
    24	  - Pages Router
    25	  - Proxy
    26	  - Client
    27	  - Server
    28	  - It just works!
    29	- supabase-ssr. A package to configure Supabase Auth to use cookies
    30	- Password-based authentication block installed via the [Supabase UI Library](https://supabase.com/ui/docs/nextjs/password-based-auth)
    31	- Styling with [Tailwind CSS](https://tailwindcss.com)
    32	- Components with [shadcn/ui](https://ui.shadcn.com/)
    33	- Optional deployment with [Supabase Vercel Integration and Vercel deploy](#deploy-your-own)
    34	  - Environment variables automatically assigned to Vercel project
    35	
    36	## Demo
    37	
    38	You can view a fully working demo at [demo-nextjs-with-supabase.vercel.app](https://demo-nextjs-with-supabase.vercel.app/).
    39	
    40	## Deploy to Vercel
    41	
    42	Vercel deployment will guide you through creating a Supabase account and project.
    43	
    44	After installation of the Supabase integration, all relevant environment variables will be assigned to the project so the deployment is fully functioning.
    45	
    46	[![Deploy with Vercel](https://vercel.com/button)](https://vercel.com/new/clone?repository-url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel%2Fnext.js%2Ftree%2Fcanary%2Fexamples%2Fwith-supabase&project-name=nextjs-with-supabase&repository-name=nextjs-with-supabase&demo-title=nextjs-with-supabase&demo-description=This+starter+configures+Supabase+Auth+to+use+cookies%2C+making+the+user%27s+session+available+throughout+the+entire+Next.js+app+-+Client+Components%2C+Server+Components%2C+Route+Handlers%2C+Server+Actions+and+Middleware.&demo-url=https%3A%2F%2Fdemo-nextjs-with-supabase.vercel.app%2F&external-id=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel%2Fnext.js%2Ftree%2Fcanary%2Fexamples%2Fwith-supabase&demo-image=https%3A%2F%2Fdemo-nextjs-with-supabase.vercel.app%2Fopengraph-image.png)
    47	
    48	The above will also clone the Starter kit to your GitHub, you can clone that locally and develop locally.
    49	
    50	If you wish to just develop locally and not deploy to Vercel, [follow the steps below](#clone-and-run-locally).
    51	
    52	## Clone and run locally
    53	
    54	1. You'll first need a Supabase project which can be made [via the Supabase dashboard](https://database.new)
    55	
    56	2. Create a Next.js app using the Supabase Starter template npx command
    57	
    58	   ```bash
    59	   npx create-next-app --example with-supabase with-supabase-app
    60	   ```
    61	
    62	   ```bash
    63	   yarn create next-app --example with-supabase with-supabase-app
    64	   ```
    65	
    66	   ```bash
    67	   pnpm create next-app --example with-supabase with-supabase-app
    68	   ```
    69	
    70	3. Use `cd` to change into the app's directory
    71	
    72	   ```bash
    73	   cd with-supabase-app
    74	   ```
    75	
    76	4. Rename `.env.example` to `.env.local` and update the following:
    77	
    78	  ```env
    79	  NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=[INSERT SUPABASE PROJECT URL]
    80	  NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=[INSERT SUPABASE PROJECT API PUBLISHABLE OR ANON KEY]
    81	  ```
    82	  > [!NOTE]
    83	  > This example uses `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`, which refers to Supabase's new **publishable** key format.
    84	  > Both legacy **anon** keys and new **publishable** keys can be used with this variable name during the transition period. Supabase's dashboard may show `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`; its value can be used in this example.
    85	  > See the [full announcement](https://github.com/orgs/supabase/discussions/29260) for more information.
    86	
    87	  Both `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL` and `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` can be found in [your Supabase project's API settings](https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/_?showConnect=true)
    88	
    89	5. You can now run the Next.js local development server:
    90	
    91	   ```bash
    92	   npm run dev
    93	   ```
    94	
    95	   The starter kit should now be running on [localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000/).
    96	
    97	6. This template comes with the default shadcn/ui style initialized. If you instead want other ui.shadcn styles, delete `components.json` and [re-install shadcn/ui](https://ui.shadcn.com/docs/installation/next)
    98	
    99	> Check out [the docs for Local Development](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/getting-started/local-development) to also run Supabase locally.
   100	
   101	## Feedback and issues
   102

    14	  source: string;
    15	  model: string | null;
    16	  reasoningEffort: string | null;
    17	  generatedAt: string | null;
    18	  refreshScheduleEt: string | null;

    21	const TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES = new Set([
    22	  "trusted-live-pull",
    23	  "trusted-authority-pull",
    24	  "ai-daily-refresh",
    25	  "chatgpt-pro-subscription-refresh",
    26	]);

    28	const SNAPSHOT_LOADERS: Record<string, () => Promise<unknown>> = {
    29	  "app/config/dashboard-risk-factors-ai.json": async () =>
    30	    (await import("@/app/config/dashboard-risk-factors-ai.json")).default,
    31	  "app/config/strategy-posture-ai.json": async () =>
    32	    (await import("@/app/config/strategy-posture-ai.json")).default,
    33	  "app/config/sentiment-overview-ai.json": async () =>
    34	    (await import("@/app/config/sentiment-overview-ai.json")).default,

    36	    (await import("@/app/config/legislation-feed-ai.json")).default,

    40	
    41	function coerceSnapshot<T extends object>(parsed: unknown): (T & AiSnapshotMeta) | null {
    42	  if (!parsed || typeof parsed !== "object") return null;
    43	  const candidate = parsed as T & Partial<AiSnapshotMeta>;
    44	  if (typeof candidate.generatedAt !== "string" || candidate.generatedAt.trim().length === 0) return null;
    45	  if (typeof candidate.model !== "string" || candidate.model.trim().length === 0) return null;
    46	  if (typeof candidate.reasoningEffort !== "string" || candidate.reasoningEffort.trim().length === 0) return null;
    47	  const snapshotSource =
    48	    typeof candidate.source === "string" ? candidate.source.trim().toLowerCase() : "";
    49	  if (!TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES.has(snapshotSource)) return null;
    50	  return candidate as T & AiSnapshotMeta;
    51	}
    52	
    53	export async function readAiSnapshot<T extends object>(
    54	  relativePathFromRepoRoot: string,
    55	): Promise<(T & AiSnapshotMeta) | null> {
    56	  try {
    57	    const loader = SNAPSHOT_LOADERS[relativePathFromRepoRoot];
    58	    if (loader) {
    59	      const imported = await loader();
    60	      const validated = coerceSnapshot<T>(imported);
    61	      if (validated) return validated;
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    const fullPath = path.join(
    65	      /* turbopackIgnore: true */ process.cwd(),
    66	      relativePathFromRepoRoot,
    67	    );
    68	    const raw = await readFile(fullPath, "utf8");
    69	    return coerceSnapshot<T>(JSON.parse(raw));
    70	  } catch {
    71	    return null;
    72	  }
    73	}
    74	
    75	export function toAiEnvelopeMeta(snapshot: AiSnapshotMeta | null): AiEnvelopeMeta {
    76	  return {
    77	    enabled: Boolean(snapshot),
    78	    source: snapshot?.source ?? "none",
    79	    model: snapshot?.model ?? null,
    80	    reasoningEffort: snapshot?.reasoningEffort ?? null,
    81	    generatedAt: snapshot?.generatedAt ?? null,
    82	    refreshScheduleEt: snapshot?.refreshScheduleEt ?? null,
    83	  };
    84	}

    46	  return dateStr.slice(0, 10) as unknown as Time;

    48	
    49	function computeVolatility(bars: ZlPriceBar[]): string {
    50	  const recent = bars.slice(-20);
    51	  if (recent.length < 2) return "--";
    52	  const returns: number[] = [];
    53	  for (let i = 1; i < recent.length; i++) {
    54	    returns.push(Math.log(recent[i].close / recent[i - 1].close));
    55	  }
    56	  const mean = returns.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / returns.length;
    57	  const variance =
    58	    returns.reduce((a, b) => a + (b - mean) ** 2, 0) / returns.length;
    59	  return (Math.sqrt(variance) * Math.sqrt(252) * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";
    60	}
    61	
    62	function computeSmaData(candles: CandlestickData<Time>[], period: number): { time: Time; value: number }[] {
    63	  if (candles.length < period) return [];
    64	
    65	  const result: { time: Time; value: number }[] = [];
    66	  let rollingSum = 0;
    67	
    68	  for (let i = 0; i < candles.length; i += 1) {
    69	    rollingSum += candles[i].close;
    70	    if (i >= period) {
    71	      rollingSum -= candles[i - period].close;
    72	    }
    73	    if (i >= period - 1) {
    74	      result.push({
    75	        time: candles[i].time,
    76	        value: rollingSum / period,
    77	      });
    78	    }
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  return result;
    82	}

    84	export function ZlCandlestickChart({
    85	  height = "70vh",
    86	  targetZones = [],
    87	}: {
    88	  height?: string | number;
    89	  targetZones?: TargetZone[];
    90	}) {

    96	
    97	  const [bars, setBars] = useState<ZlPriceBar[]>([]);
    98	  const [lastPrice, setLastPrice] = useState<number | null>(null);
    99	  const [priceChange, setPriceChange] = useState(0);
   100	  const [highPrice, setHighPrice] = useState<number | null>(null);
   101	  const [lowPrice, setLowPrice] = useState<number | null>(null);
   102	  const [volatility, setVolatility] = useState("--");
   103	
   104	  // Fetch daily bars
   105	  useEffect(() => {
   106	    async function fetchBars() {
   107	      try {
   108	        const res = await fetch("/api/zl/price-1d", { cache: "no-store" });
   109	        if (!res.ok) return;
   110	        const json = await res.json();
   111	        if (!json.data || json.data.length === 0) return;
   112	
   113	        const parsed: ZlPriceBar[] = json.data.map(
   114	          (d: Record<string, unknown>) => ({
   115	            symbol: String(d.symbol),
   116	            tradeDate: String(d.tradeDate),
   117	            open: Number(d.open),
   118	            high: Number(d.high),
   119	            low: Number(d.low),
   120	            close: Number(d.close),
   121	            volume: Number(d.volume),
   122	          }),
   123	        );
   124	
   125	        setBars(parsed);
   126	
   127	        const latest = parsed[parsed.length - 1];
   128	        const prev = parsed[parsed.length - 2];
   129	        setLastPrice(latest.close);
   130	        setHighPrice(latest.high);
   131	        setLowPrice(latest.low);
   132	        setVolatility(computeVolatility(parsed));
   133	
   134	        if (prev) {
   135	          setPriceChange(((latest.close - prev.close) / prev.close) * 100);
   136	        }
   137	      } catch {
   138	        /* fail silently — chart stays empty */
   139	      }

   259	    series.attachPrimitive(pivotPrimitive);
   260	    if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {

   262	    }
   263	
   264	    // Forecast target zones should be projected near the most recent bars, not full-width.
   265	    if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {
   266	      const targetStartIndex = Math.max(0, candleData.length - 16);
   267	      const targetStartTime = candleData[targetStartIndex]?.time;
   268	      forecastTargetsPrimitive.setTargetZones(targetZones, targetStartTime);
   269	    }
   270	
   271	    // Fib rendering: anchored start, pivot zone fill, and structural-break lock.
   272	    const fibCandles: CandleData[] = bars.map((b, idx) => ({
   273	      time: idx,
   274	      open: b.open,
   275	      high: b.high,
   276	      low: b.low,
   277	      close: b.close,
   278	      volume: b.volume,
   279	    }));
   280	
   281	    const currentPrice = bars[bars.length - 1]?.close;
   282	    let fibResult = fibLockedRef.current;
   283	    if (
   284	      !fibResult ||
   285	      currentPrice == null ||
   286	      currentPrice > fibResult.anchorHigh ||
   287	      currentPrice < fibResult.anchorLow
   288	    ) {
   289	      fibResult = calculateFibonacciMultiPeriod(fibCandles);
   290	      fibLockedRef.current = fibResult;
   291	    }
   292	
   293	    if (fibResult) {
   294	      const anchorIdx = Math.min(
   295	        fibResult.anchorHighBarIndex,
   296	        fibResult.anchorLowBarIndex,
   297	      );
   298	      const anchorStartTime = candleData[anchorIdx]?.time;
   299	      pivotPrimitive.setFibResult(fibResult, anchorStartTime);
   300	    } else {
   301	      pivotPrimitive.setFibResult(null);
   302	    }
   303	
   304	    // Set initial visible range: last N bars + right padding
   305	    if (!fitCalledRef.current && candleData.length > 0) {
   306	      const total = candleData.length;
   307	      const visible = Math.min(INITIAL_VISIBLE_BARS, total);
   308	      chart.timeScale().setVisibleLogicalRange({
   309	        from: Math.max(0, total - visible),
   310	        to: total - 1 + RIGHT_PADDING_BARS,
   311	      });
   312	      fitCalledRef.current = true;
   313	    }
   314	
   315	    // Responsive resize
   316	    let disposed = false;
   317	    const observer = new ResizeObserver((entries) => {
   318	      if (disposed || !entries[0]) return;
   319	      const { width, height: h } = entries[0].contentRect;
   320	      try {
   321	        chart.applyOptions({ width, height: h });
   322	      } catch {
   323	        /* disposed */
   324	      }
   325	    });
   326	    observer.observe(containerRef.current);
   327	
   328	    return () => {
   329	      disposed = true;
   330	      observer.disconnect();
   331	      try {
   332	        if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {
   333	          series.detachPrimitive(forecastTargetsPrimitive);
   334	        }
   335	        series.detachPrimitive(pivotPrimitive);
   336	        chart.remove();
   337	      } catch {
   338	        /* disposed */
   339	      }
   340	    };
   341	  }, [bars, targetZones]);
   342	
   343	  const changeColor = priceChange >= 0 ? "#26C6DA" : "#EC0000";
   344	
   345	  return (
   346	    <div
   347	      className="relative w-full rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-white/5 flex flex-col"
   348	      style={{
   349	        background: "linear-gradient(180deg, #131722 0%, #0d1117 100%)",

   359	              ZL1!

     1	"use client"
     2	
     3	import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react"
     4	
     5	interface ForecastTarget {
     6	  id: string
     7	  horizonDays: number
     8	  horizonLabel: string
     9	  priceLow: number | null
    10	  priceHigh: number | null
    11	  oofPrice: number | null
    12	  coveragePct: number | null
    13	  isMissing?: boolean
    14	}
    15	
    16	const BIN_COUNT = 11
    17	const AG_HORIZON_DAYS = [30, 90, 180] as const
    18	
    19	function horizonLabel(days: number): string {
    20	  if (days === 30) return "1M"
    21	  if (days === 90) return "3M"
    22	  if (days === 180) return "6M"
    23	  return `${days}d`
    24	}
    25	
    26	function clamp(v: number, min: number, max: number): number {
    27	  return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, v))
    28	}
    29	
    30	function cellAlpha(price: number, t: ForecastTarget): number {
    31	  if (t.priceLow === null || t.priceHigh === null || t.oofPrice === null) {
    32	    return 0.08
    33	  }
    34	
    35	  const low = Math.min(t.priceLow, t.priceHigh)
    36	  const high = Math.max(t.priceLow, t.priceHigh)
    37	  const halfWidth = Math.max((high - low) / 2, 0.1)
    38	  const centerDist = Math.abs(price - t.oofPrice) / halfWidth
    39	  const insideZone = price >= low && price <= high
    40	
    41	  if (insideZone) {
    42	    return clamp(1 - centerDist * 0.75, 0.25, 1)
    43	  }
    44	
    45	  const outsideDist = Math.abs(price - t.oofPrice) / (halfWidth * 2.5)
    46	  return clamp(0.18 - outsideDist * 0.12, 0.04, 0.18)
    47	}
    48	
    49	export function ProbabilitySurface() {
    50	  const [targets, setTargets] = useState<ForecastTarget[]>([])
    51	  const [asOfDate, setAsOfDate] = useState<string | null>(null)
    52	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
    53	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)
    54	
    55	  useEffect(() => {
    56	    let cancelled = false
    57	
    58	    async function loadTargets() {
    59	      setLoading(true)
    60	      setError(null)
    61	      try {
    62	        const res = await fetch("/api/zl/forecast-targets", { cache: "no-store" })
    63	        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`)
    64	        const json = await res.json()
    65	        if (cancelled) return
    66	        setTargets(
    67	          (json.targets ?? [])
    68	            .filter(
    69	              (t: ForecastTarget) =>
    70	                AG_HORIZON_DAYS.includes(t?.horizonDays as (typeof AG_HORIZON_DAYS)[number]) &&
    71	                typeof t?.horizonDays === "number" &&
    72	                typeof t?.priceLow === "number" &&
    73	                typeof t?.priceHigh === "number" &&
    74	                typeof t?.oofPrice === "number",
    75	            )
    76	            .map((t: ForecastTarget) => ({
    77	              ...t,
    78	              horizonLabel: horizonLabel(t.horizonDays),
    79	            }))
    80	            .sort((a: ForecastTarget, b: ForecastTarget) => a.horizonDays - b.horizonDays),
    81	        )
    82	        setAsOfDate(json.asOfDate ?? null)
    83	      } catch (e) {
    84	        if (cancelled) return
    85	        setError(e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load target zones")
    86	      } finally {
    87	        if (!cancelled) setLoading(false)
    88	      }
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    loadTargets()
    92	    return () => { cancelled = true }
    93	  }, [])
    94	
    95	  const priceBins = useMemo(() => {
    96	    const resolvedTargets = targets.filter(
    97	      (t) => t.priceLow !== null && t.priceHigh !== null && t.oofPrice !== null,
    98	    )
    99	    if (resolvedTargets.length === 0) return [] as number[]
   100	
   101	    const low = Math.min(...resolvedTargets.map((t) => Math.min(t.priceLow!, t.priceHigh!)))
   102	    const high = Math.max(...resolvedTargets.map((t) => Math.max(t.priceLow!, t.priceHigh!)))
   103	    if (!Number.isFinite(low) || !Number.isFinite(high)) return [] as number[]
   104	
   105	    const span = Math.max(high - low, 1)
   106	    const min = low - span * 0.05
   107	    const max = high + span * 0.05
   108	    const step = (max - min) / (BIN_COUNT - 1)
   109	
   110	    return Array.from(
   111	      { length: BIN_COUNT },
   112	      (_, idx) => Number((max - idx * step).toFixed(2)),
   113	    )
   114	  }, [targets])
   115	
   116	  const displayTargets = useMemo(() => {
   117	    const byHorizon = new Map<number, ForecastTarget>()
   118	    for (const t of targets) byHorizon.set(t.horizonDays, t)
   119	
   120	    return AG_HORIZON_DAYS.map((horizonDays) => {
   121	      const resolved = byHorizon.get(horizonDays)
   122	      if (resolved) return resolved
   123	
   124	      return {
   125	        id: `missing-${horizonDays}`,
   126	        horizonDays,
   127	        horizonLabel: horizonLabel(horizonDays),
   128	        priceLow: null,
   129	        priceHigh: null,
   130	        oofPrice: null,
   131	        coveragePct: null,
   132	        isMissing: true,
   133	      } satisfies ForecastTarget
   134	    })
   135	  }, [targets])
   136	
   137	  const gridTemplateColumns = `56px repeat(${Math.max(displayTargets.length, 1)}, minmax(0,1fr))`
   138	
   139	  return (
   140	    <div className="w-full bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-white/5 rounded-xl p-6 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
   141	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
   142	        <div>
   143	          <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-white uppercase tracking-wider">
   144	            L3 Probability Surface
   145	          </h3>
   146	          <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">
   147	            Real target zone density from latest AG trading-model forecast (1M/3M/6M)
   148	            {asOfDate ? ` (as of ${asOfDate})` : ""}
   149	          </p>
   150	        </div>
   151	        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-[10px] text-slate-500">
   152	          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
   153	            <span className="inline-block w-2 h-2 rounded-[1px] bg-cyan-400/90" />
   154	            High
   155	          </div>
   156	          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
   157	            <span className="inline-block w-2 h-2 rounded-[1px] bg-cyan-400/20" />
   158	            Low
   159	          </div>
   160	        </div>
   161	      </div>
   162	
   163	      {loading && (
   164	        <div className="mt-6 text-sm text-slate-400">Loading forecast density...</div>
   165	      )}
   166	
   167	      {!loading && error && (
   168	        <div className="mt-6 text-sm text-red-400">Failed to load probability data: {error}</div>
   169	      )}
   170	
   171	      {!loading && !error && targets.length === 0 && (
   172	        <div className="mt-6 text-sm text-slate-400">
   173	          No production target zones available yet. This view populates automatically once forecast rows are present.
   174	        </div>
   175	      )}
   176	
   177	      {!loading && !error && targets.length > 0 && (
   178	        <div className="mt-6 space-y-2">
   179	          <div className="grid gap-1" style={{ gridTemplateColumns }}>
   180	            <div />
   181	            {displayTargets.map((t) => (
   182	              <div key={`h-${t.id}`} className="text-center text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono">
   183	                <div>{t.horizonLabel}</div>
   184	                {t.isMissing && (
   185	                  <div className="text-[9px] text-slate-600">pending</div>

   187	              </div>
   188	            ))}
   189	
   190	            {priceBins.map((price) => (
   191	              <React.Fragment key={`row-${price}`}>
   192	                <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-600 font-mono pr-2 text-right">
   193	                  ${price.toFixed(2)}
   194	                </div>
   195	                {displayTargets.map((t) => {
   196	                  const alpha = cellAlpha(price, t)
   197	                  const title = t.isMissing
   198	                    ? `${t.horizonLabel} | awaiting forecast rows`
   199	                    : `${t.horizonLabel} | zone $${t.priceLow!.toFixed(2)}-$${t.priceHigh!.toFixed(2)} | median $${t.oofPrice!.toFixed(2)}`
   200	                  return (

   207	                      }}
   208	                      title={title}

   221	              </div>

    48	        """[Req: code-derived — REQ-003] all ingest writers should share one status vocabulary."""
    49	        helper = read_text("lib/server/ingest-run.ts")
    50	        sql_intraday = read_text("supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql")
    51	        sql_fill = read_text("supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql")
    52	
    53	        helper_statuses = set(re.findall(r'status:\s*"([A-Z_]+)"', helper))
    54	        sql_statuses = set(re.findall(r"status\s*:=\s*'([a-z_]+)'", sql_intraday + "\n" + sql_fill))
    55	        self.assertTrue(helper_statuses, "Expected TS helper status literals to be present.")
    56	        self.assertTrue(sql_statuses, "Expected SQL status literals to be present.")
    57	
    58	        normalized_sql = {s.upper() for s in sql_statuses}
    59	        self.assertSetEqual(
    60	            helper_statuses,
    61	            normalized_sql,
    62	            "REQ-003 violation: SQL and TS status vocabularies are not canonicalized to one set.",
    63	        )

   214	class BoundaryAndEdgeCaseTests(unittest.TestCase):
   215	    def test_boundary_intraday_tables_exist_in_migration_contract(self) -> None:
   216	        """[Req: inferred — from mkt schema tables] both intraday table levels exist."""

   221	    def test_boundary_horizon_allowlist_parity_across_routes(self) -> None:

   225	        targets = read_text("app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts")

.github/skills/quality-playbook/references/phase2_generation_guide.md:91:**Exception — `citation_semantic_check.json` uses `reviews` instead of `records`** per `schemas.md` §9.1. Same wrapper shape, different array key; the records inside are Council review entries, not REQ/UC/BUG records. If you find yourself writing `records` into `citation_semantic_check.json`, stop and re-read schemas.md §9 — the gate rejects this file as a manifest-wrapper violation (schemas.md §10 invariant #13) when the key is wrong.

usage: reference_docs_ingest [-h] [target]

Ingest plaintext documentation from ``reference_docs/``. v1.5.2 collapses the
v1.5.1 ``formal_docs/`` + ``informal_docs/`` split into a single
``reference_docs/`` tree: * Files at the top level of ``reference_docs/`` are
Tier 4 context (AI chats, design notes, retrospectives). They are loaded into
Phase 1 prompts as background; no manifest record is written. * Files under
``reference_docs/cite/`` are citable sources (specs, RFCs, API contracts).
Each produces a ``FORMAL_DOC`` record in ``quality/formal_docs_manifest.json``
with a mechanical citation excerpt. The manifest file name stays
``formal_docs_manifest.json`` for backward-compatibility with downstream gate
logic and existing benchmark artifacts. Schema unchanged; only source
directory changes. Optional in-file tier marker on the first non-blank line of
a ``cite/`` file preserves the internal Tier 1 / Tier 2 distinction: <!-- qpb-
tier: 2 --> # qpb-tier: 2 A tier marker is considered *present* in the file if
any line contains the substring ``qpb-tier``. If present, the marker must
match the expected regex and must appear on the first non-blank line —
otherwise ingest fails. Files with no ``qpb-tier`` substring anywhere default
to Tier 1. This default-Tier-1 behavior for untagged files is intentional and
out of scope for v1.5.2; the tiering model for untagged content is a deferred
design question. Top-level (Tier 4) files ignore the marker.

positional arguments:
  target      Target repo path (default: cwd)

options:
  -h, --help  show this help message and exit

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# Probe 1 (confirmation probe, expected FAIL assertion):
# Claim under test (REQ-001): trusted-site fill failure path should update the same run_id.
# Evidence lines: scripts/fill_site_with_trusted_data.py lines 1848-1853 currently use a
# subquery by job_name instead of run_id.
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path

text = Path("scripts/fill_site_with_trusted_data.py").read_text(encoding="utf-8")
start = text.rindex("except Exception as err")
end = text.index("finally:", start)
except_block = text[start:end]

# Expected-failing assertion confirms BUG-010 on current source.
try:
    assert "WHERE run_id = %s" in except_block, (
        "line 1848 currently is not `WHERE run_id = %s`; failure-path update is not keyed to local run_id"
    )
except AssertionError as exc:
    print(f"PROBE-REQ001-FAILPATH: EXPECTED_FAIL confirmed -> {exc}")
else:
    raise SystemExit("PROBE-REQ001-FAILPATH unexpectedly passed; re-triage BUG-010")
PY

# Probe 2 (rejection proof, passing assertion):
# Claim under test (auditor singleton): risk-factors API gives no fallback observability cues.
# Evidence lines: app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts lines 860-867 include explicit ai.enabled/source/meta.
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path

text = Path("app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts").read_text(encoding="utf-8")
assert "enabled: Boolean(aiSnapshot)" in text, "line 861 missing ai.enabled indicator"
assert "source: aiSnapshot?.source ?? \"weekly-db-plus-ai-snapshot\"" in text, (
    "line 862 missing fallback source marker"
)
assert "generatedAt: aiSnapshot?.generatedAt ?? responseGeneratedAt" in text, (
    "line 865 missing generatedAt fallback marker"
)
print("PROBE-REQ004-AI-META: PASS (fallback observability markers are present in API envelope)")

+- Severity: MEDIUM

+### BUG-006: Probability surface consumes divergent forecast-targets contract path
+- Source: Spec Audit (Council Triaged)
+- Primary requirement: REQ-002
+- Severity: MEDIUM
+- divergence_type: code-spec
+- Disposition: code-fix
+- fix_type: code
+- Location: components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:62, components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:67-68, components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:82
+- Spec basis: REQ-002 requires one stable envelope contract (or one explicit adapter) across equivalent forecast-target consumers.
+- Expected behavior: Probability surface consumes canonical envelope semantics used by sibling forecast-target surfaces.
+- Actual behavior: Component fetches `/api/zl/forecast-targets` and parses route-specific keys (`json.targets`, `json.asOfDate`), preserving client-level contract divergence.
+- Evidence: `components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:62`, `components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:67-68`, `components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:82`, `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.out.txt` (`PROBE-REQ002-SURFACE-CONTRACT`).

+- Fix patch: quality/patches/BUG-006-fix.patch
+- Disposition rationale: Divergence is consumer-side contract binding, not data availability.
+- Proposed fix: Rebind ProbabilitySurface to canonical target-zones envelope (or shared adapter) and remove route-specific parsing.

+### BUG-006: Probability surface consumes divergent forecast-targets contract path
+- Source: Spec Audit (Council Triaged)
+- Primary requirement: REQ-002
+- Severity: MEDIUM
+- divergence_type: code-spec
+- Disposition: code-fix
+- fix_type: code

+- Actual behavior: Component fetches `/api/zl/forecast-targets` and parses route-specific keys (`json.targets`, `json.asOfDate`), preserving client-level contract divergence.

+- Fix patch: quality/patches/BUG-006-fix.patch
+- Disposition rationale: Divergence is consumer-side contract binding, not data availability.
+- Proposed fix: Rebind ProbabilitySurface to canonical target-zones envelope (or shared adapter) and remove route-specific parsing.

+### BUG-006: Probability surface consumes divergent forecast-targets contract path

+- Primary requirement: REQ-002
+- Severity: MEDIUM

+- divergence_type: code-spec

+### BUG-006: Probability surface consumes divergent forecast-targets contract path
+- Source: Spec Audit (Council Triaged)
+- Primary requirement: REQ-002
+- Severity: MEDIUM
+- divergence_type: code-spec
+- Disposition: code-fix
+- fix_type: code
+- Location: components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:62, components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:67-68, components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:82
+- Spec basis: REQ-002 requires one stable envelope contract (or one explicit adapter) across equivalent forecast-target consumers.
+- Expected behavior: Probability surface consumes canonical envelope semantics used by sibling forecast-target surfaces.
+- Actual behavior: Component fetches `/api/zl/forecast-targets` and parses route-specific keys (`json.targets`, `json.asOfDate`), preserving client-level contract divergence.

+- Fix patch: quality/patches/BUG-006-fix.patch
+- Disposition rationale: Divergence is consumer-side contract binding, not data availability.
+- Proposed fix: Rebind ProbabilitySurface to canonical target-zones envelope (or shared adapter) and remove route-specific parsing.
